# What is GoldRush - GoldRush API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://goldrush.dev/docs/overview#content-area)

[GoldRush API Documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=97917fde1507b0c14e79b83959fe1160)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=5bd4f921dcc81186bf369e7b33ec5734)](https://goldrush.dev/docs)

Navigation

Learn about GoldRush

What is GoldRush

[Overview](https://goldrush.dev/docs/overview)
[Foundational API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/overview)
[Streaming API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/overview)
[Chains](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/overview)

On this page

*   [Pick your Use Case](https://goldrush.dev/docs/overview#pick-your-use-case)
    

Whether you’re building a DeFi dashboard, a wallet, a trading bot, an AI agent or a compliance platform, our Blockchain Data APIs provide fast, accurate, and developer-friendly access to the essential onchain data you need. GoldRush indexes the entire chain data, from the genesis block to the latest block, across multiple data types: balances, transactions, logs, internal transfers, pricing, and smart contract events. You get complete, verifiable coverage without running your own node infrastructure.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/overview#pick-your-use-case)

Pick your Use Case
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

GoldRush offers two core self-serve products that can be used independently or together to power your application.

[Foundational API\
----------------\
\
Access structured historical blockchain data across 100+ chains using REST APIs. Get token balances, transaction histories, decoded event logs, NFT assets, token holders and more.  \
  \
**Use cases: Wallets, portfolio trackers, crypto accounting & tax tools, and DeFi dashboards.**\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api)
[Streaming API\
-------------\
\
Subscribe to real-time blockchain events with sub-second latency using GraphQL over WebSockets. Track token transfers, DEX activity, wallet movements, and OHLCV candlestick data across fast chains like Base and Solana.  \
  \
**Use cases: Trading bots & dashboards, gaming, and AI Agents.**\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api)

[Powered by GoldRush](https://goldrush.dev/docs/powered-by-goldrush)

Ctrl+I

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

# GoldRush SDKs - GoldRush API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-sdks#content-area)

[GoldRush API Documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=97917fde1507b0c14e79b83959fe1160)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=5bd4f921dcc81186bf369e7b33ec5734)](https://goldrush.dev/docs)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Components

GoldRush SDKs

[Overview](https://goldrush.dev/docs/overview)
[Foundational API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/overview)
[Streaming API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/overview)
[Chains](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/overview)

The GoldRush SDKs are official open-source client libraries that wrap around the GoldRush APIs, providing developers with more seamless options to access onchain data. The following client libraries are currently provided:

1.  **TypeScript:** [https://www.npmjs.com/package/@covalenthq/client-sdk](https://www.npmjs.com/package/@covalenthq/client-sdk)
    
2.  **Python:** [https://pypi.org/project/covalent-api-sdk/](https://pypi.org/project/covalent-api-sdk/)
    

[Changelog](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog)
[GoldRush MCP Server](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-mcp-server)

⌘I

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/faq#general-questions)

General Questions
-------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/faq#what-is-the-goldrush-api)

What is the GoldRush API?

GoldRush offers the most comprehensive Blockchain Data API suite for developers, analysts, and enterprises.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/faq#what-can-i-do-with-the-goldrush-api)

What can I do with the GoldRush API?

The GoldRush API provdes fast, accurate, and developer-friendly access to the essential onchain data for building DeFi dashboards, wallets, trading bots, AI Agents, tax and compliance platforms.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/faq#do-i-need-api-keys-to-use-goldrush)

Do I need API keys to use GoldRush?

Yes, you need an API key to access the GoldRush API. Your API Key is available on the [GoldRush platform](https://goldrush.dev/docs/platform)
 when you sign up for an account.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/faq#if-a-client-asks-how-to-verify-that-goldrush-api-is-real-time-or-low-latency,-how-can-we-demonstrate-or-prove-that)

If a client asks how to verify that GoldRush API is real-time or low-latency, how can we demonstrate or prove that?

You can demonstrate real-time or low-latency capabilities through:

*   Timestamp validation: Pull `/v1/{chain_id}/block_v2/latest/` and compare the block timestamp with the current time (should be sub-second to a few seconds behind depending on chain).
*   Latency benchmarks: Use tools like curl or Postman to measure API response time. GoldRush’s streaming endpoints often respond in under 400ms for supported chains.
*   Streaming demos: If using the Streaming API, show live updates of token transfers or block finality in dev dashboards.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/faq#besides-the-common-401,-402,-and-429-error-codes,-are-there-any-other-error-responses-we-should-be-aware-of)

Besides the common 401, 402, and 429 error codes, are there any other error responses we should be aware of?

Yes. Additional error codes include:

*   `400 Bad Request` – Invalid parameters or malformed request.
*   `402 Payment Required` – Alloted credits exceeded and need to enable Flex Credits or upgrade subscription tier.
*   `403 Forbidden` – API key is valid but not authorized for the resource.
*   `404 Not Found` – Endpoint or data not available (e.g. unsupported chain).
*   `500 Internal Server Error` – Unexpected failure on Covalent’s side.
*   `503 Service Unavailable` – Maintenance or backend issue.

Each error includes a descriptive JSON body for debugging.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/faq#foundational-api-questions)

Foundational API Questions
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/faq#what-is-the-rate-limit-for-api-calls)

What is the rate limit for API calls?

The GoldRush Foundational API enforces rate limits based on the user’s plan:

*   14-day Free Trial plan: 4 requests per second (RPS), 25,000 API credits.
*   Professional plan: 50 RPS.
*   Inner Circle plan: Custom limits, typically up to 100 RPS or higher, based on SLAs.

Rate limits are enforced per API key and IP, and requests exceeding limits receive a `429 Too Many Requests` error.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/faq#streaming-api-questions)

Streaming API Questions
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/faq#how-does-the-streaming-api-work)

How does the Streaming API work?

The Streaming API uses WebSocket connections to provide real-time updates about blockchain events. It maintains a persistent connection and pushes structured data to subscribed clients as events occur.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/faq#what-types-of-events-can-i-subscribe-to)

What types of events can I subscribe to?

See all available streams on the [Streaming API Overview](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/overview)
.

[Powered by GoldRush](https://goldrush.dev/docs/powered-by-goldrush)
[Changelog](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog)

# GoldRush MCP Server - GoldRush API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-mcp-server#content-area)

[GoldRush API Documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=97917fde1507b0c14e79b83959fe1160)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=5bd4f921dcc81186bf369e7b33ec5734)](https://goldrush.dev/docs)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Components

GoldRush MCP Server

[Overview](https://goldrush.dev/docs/overview)
[Foundational API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/overview)
[Streaming API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/overview)
[Chains](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/overview)

On this page

*   [Setup Instructions](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-mcp-server#setup-instructions)
    
*   [Step 1: Installation](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-mcp-server#step-1%3A-installation)
    
*   [Step 2: Configure with MCP clients](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-mcp-server#step-2%3A-configure-with-mcp-clients)
    
*   [Step 3: Programmatic Usage](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-mcp-server#step-3%3A-programmatic-usage)
    
*   [Available Tools](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-mcp-server#available-tools)
    
*   [Available Resources](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-mcp-server#available-resources)
    
*   [Example LLM Interaction](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-mcp-server#example-llm-interaction)
    

The GoldRush MCP Server provides a [Model Context Protocol (MCP)](https://modelcontextprotocol.io/)
 implementation that exposes GoldRush APIs as MCP resources and tools. It enables LLMs to interact with blockchain data across multiple chains.

You’ll need a GoldRush API key to use this server.

[Get Started\
-----------\
\
Sign up for a free API key to get started with GoldRush.](https://goldrush.dev/platform/auth/register/)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-mcp-server#setup-instructions)

Setup Instructions
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-mcp-server#step-1:-installation)

Step 1: Installation

No installation is needed as the server can be run directly using `npx`.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-mcp-server#step-2:-configure-with-mcp-clients)

Step 2: Configure with MCP clients

1

Usage with Claude Desktop

Add this to your `claude_desktop_config.json`:

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "mcpServers": {
        "goldrush": {
          "command": "npx",
          "args": [\
            "-y",\
            "@covalenthq/goldrush-mcp-server@latest"\
          ],
          "env": {
            "GOLDRUSH_API_KEY": "YOUR_API_KEY_HERE"
          }
        }
      }
    }   
    

For more details, follow the official [MCP Quickstart for Claude Desktop Users](https://modelcontextprotocol.io/quickstart/user)
.

2

Usage with Claude Code CLI

Copy

Ask AI

    $ claude mcp add goldrush -e GOLDRUSH_API_KEY=<YOUR_API_KEY_HERE> -- npx @covalenthq/goldrush-mcp-server
    

For more details, see [Set up Model Context Protocol (MCP)](https://docs.anthropic.com/en/docs/agents-and-tools/claude-code/tutorials#set-up-model-context-protocol-mcp)
.

3

Usage with Cursor

1.  Open Cursor Settings
2.  Go to Features > MCP
3.  Click + Add new global MCP server
4.  Add this to your `~/.cursor/mcp.json`:

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "mcpServers": {
        "goldrush": {
          "command": "npx",
          "args": [\
            "-y",\
            "@covalenthq/goldrush-mcp-server@latest"\
          ],
          "env": {
            "GOLDRUSH_API_KEY": "YOUR_API_KEY_HERE"
          }
        }
      }
    }   
    

For project-specific configuration, add the above to a `.cursor/mcp.json` file in your project directory.

4

Usage with Windsurf

Add this to your `~/.codeium/windsurf/mcp_config.json` file:

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "mcpServers": {
        "goldrush": {
          "command": "npx",
          "args": [\
            "-y",\
            "@covalenthq/goldrush-mcp-server@latest"\
          ],
          "env": {
            "GOLDRUSH_API_KEY": "YOUR_API_KEY_HERE"
          }
        }
      }
    }   
    

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-mcp-server#step-3:-programmatic-usage)

Step 3: Programmatic Usage

The server is designed to be started as a subprocess by an MCP client. Here’s an example using the MCP TypeScript SDK:

Copy

Ask AI

    import { Client } from "@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/client/index.js";
    import { StdioClientTransport } from "@modelcontextprotocol/sdk/client/stdio.js";
    
    const transport = new StdioClientTransport({
      command: "npx",
      args: ["-y", "@covalenthq/goldrush-mcp-server@latest"],
      env: {"GOLDRUSH_API_KEY": "your_api_key_here"}
    });
    
    const client = new Client(
      {
        name: "example-client",
        version: "1.0.0"
      },
      {
        capabilities: {
          tools: {}
        }
      }
    );
    
    await client.connect(transport);
    
    // List tools
    const resources = await client.listTools();
    const tools = await client.listTools();
    console.log("Available tools:", tools.tools.map(tool => tool.name).join(", "));
    
    // Now you can call tools
    const result = await client.callTool({
      name: "getAllChains",
      arguments: {}
    });
    
    console.log(result);
    

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-mcp-server#available-tools)

Available Tools
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The GoldRush MCP Server exposes over 50 tools for interacting with blockchain data. Here are some of the most commonly used tools:

Cross Chain

*   **multichain\_address\_activity**: Gets a summary of wallet activity across all supported blockchains.
*   **multichain\_balances**: Gets token balances for a wallet address across multiple blockchains.
*   **multichain\_transactions**: Gets transactions for multiple wallet addresses across multiple blockchains.

Balances

*   **token\_balances**: Commonly used to fetch the native and fungible (ERC20) tokens held by an address.
*   **historical\_token\_balances**: Commonly used to fetch the historical native and fungible (ERC20) tokens held by an address at a given block height or date.
*   **native\_token\_balance**: Get the native token balance (ETH, BNB, MATIC, etc.) for a specified wallet address on a blockchain.
*   **erc20\_token\_transfers**: Commonly used to render the transfer-in and transfer-out of a token along with historical prices from an address.
*   **historical\_portfolio\_value**: Commonly used to render a daily portfolio balance for an address broken down by the token.
*   **token\_holders**: Used to get a paginated list of current or historical token holders for a specified ERC20 or ERC721 token.

Transaction

*   **transaction**: Commonly used to fetch and render a single transaction including its decoded log events.
*   **transaction\_summary**: Commonly used to fetch the earliest and latest transactions, and the transaction count for a wallet.
*   **transactions\_for\_address**: Commonly used to fetch and render the most recent transactions involving an address.
*   **transactions\_for\_block**: Commonly used to fetch all transactions including their decoded log events in a block and further flag interesting wallets or transactions.

NFT

*   **nft\_for\_address**: Commonly used to get all NFTs owned by a specific wallet address on a blockchain.
*   **nft\_check\_ownership**: Commonly used to verify ownership of NFTs (including ERC-721 and ERC-1155) within a collection.

Security

*   **token\_approvals**: Commonly used to get a list of approvals across all token contracts categorized by spenders for a wallet’s assets.

Bitcoin

*   **bitcoin\_hd\_wallet\_balances**: Fetch balances for each active child address derived from a Bitcoin HD wallet.
*   **bitcoin\_non\_hd\_wallet\_balances**: Fetch Bitcoin balance for a non-HD address.
*   **bitcoin\_transactions**: Fetch transactions for a specific Bitcoin address with full transaction details.

Prices

*   **historical\_token\_prices**: Commonly used to get historic prices of a token between date ranges.
*   **gas\_prices**: Get real-time gas estimates for different transaction speeds on a specific network.

Utility

*   **log\_events\_by\_address**: Commonly used to get all the event logs emitted from a particular contract address.
*   **log\_events\_by\_topic**: Commonly used to get all event logs of the same topic hash across all contracts within a particular chain.
*   **block**: Commonly used to fetch and render a single block for a block explorer.
*   **block\_heights**: Commonly used to get all the block heights within a particular date range.

Visit our [GitHub repository](https://github.com/covalenthq/goldrush-mcp-server)
 for a complete list of tools and their parameters.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-mcp-server#available-resources)

Available Resources
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Resources are a core primitive in the Model Context Protocol that allow servers to expose data and content for use as context in LLM interactions. The GoldRush MCP Server provides both static and dynamic resources:

Static Resources

*   **config://supported-chains**: Provides a list of all blockchain networks supported by the GoldRush API
*   **config://quote-currencies**: Provides a list of all supported quote currencies for price conversions

Dynamic Resources

*   **status://all-chains**: Provides real-time synchronization status for all chains
*   **status://chain/**: Provides detailed status information for a specific chain

Dynamic resources fetch real-time data from the GoldRush API on each request, ensuring current information.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-mcp-server#example-llm-interaction)

Example LLM Interaction
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once you’ve set up the GoldRush MCP Server with your preferred LLM client, you can start asking blockchain-related questions:

*   “What are the top tokens in this Ethereum wallet: 0xeefB13C7D42eFCc655E528dA6d6F7bBcf9A2251d?”
*   “Show me the transaction history for this wallet address on Polygon.”
*   “What NFTs does this wallet own across multiple chains?”
*   “Get the gas prices for ERC20 transfers on Ethereum mainnet.”

The LLM will automatically use the appropriate GoldRush MCP tools to retrieve the blockchain data and provide you with informative responses.

[GoldRush SDKs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-sdks)

⌘I

Use Cases
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[![1750700004-goldrush-images-03](https://www.datocms-assets.com/86369/1750700004-goldrush-images-03.png)\
\
Wallet API\
----------\
\
Multichain token balances (ERC20, 721, 1155, native), token transfers and prices (spot and historical) for a wallet.\
\
API Reference](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-balances-for-address)
[![1750700004-goldrush-images-04](https://www.datocms-assets.com/86369/1750700004-goldrush-images-04.png)\
\
Activity Feed API\
-----------------\
\
Multichain historical transactions with human-readable event logs and historical prices. Includes transaction count and gas usage/spend summaries.\
\
API Reference](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-transaction-summary-for-address)
[![1750700004-goldrush-images-05](https://www.datocms-assets.com/86369/1750700004-goldrush-images-05.png)\
\
NFT API\
-------\
\
Media assets, metadata, sales, owners, trait and attribute filters, thumbnail previews.\
\
API Reference](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/get-nfts-for-address)
[![1750700004-goldrush-images-02](https://www.datocms-assets.com/86369/1750700004-goldrush-images-02.png)\
\
Bitcoin API\
-----------\
\
Bitcoin balances and transactions for x/y/zpub and non-HD addresses, including historical and spot prices.\
\
API Reference](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balance-for-address)
[![1750700004-goldrush-images-07](https://www.datocms-assets.com/86369/1750700004-goldrush-images-07.png)\
\
Security API\
------------\
\
NFT and ERC20 token allowances, including value-at-risk.\
\
API Reference](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/security/get-token-approvals-for-address)
[![1750700004-goldrush-images-08](https://www.datocms-assets.com/86369/1750700004-goldrush-images-08.png)\
\
Block Explorer API\
------------------\
\
Block details, event logs by contract address or topic hash, gas prices, token prices & holders.\
\
API Reference](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-logs)

August 13, 2025

Streaming API

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#update-pairs-stream-beta)

Update Pairs Stream (Beta)
===============================================================================================

The new Update Pairs stream delivers real-time updates for one or many DEX pairs, including price, price in USD, volume, market cap, and liquidity.

*   Supported chains: Base Mainnet, BSC Mainnet, Ethereum Mainnet
*   Supported DEXes: Uniswap V2, Uniswap V3, PancakeSwap
*   Subscribe with `updatePairs(chain_name, pair_addresses[])` over GraphQL

Note: The GoldRush Streaming API is currently in Beta. No API credits are currently charged.[Learn more](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/update-pairs)

Updated Streaming API URL
===============================================================================================

The GoldRush Streaming API URL has been updated to support authentication using the GoldRush API key.The updated URL is: `wss://gr-staging-v2.streaming.covalenthq.com/graphql`The prior URL was: `wss://gr-staging.streaming.covalenthq.com/graphql`See the [Streaming API Docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/overview)
 for more details.[Learn more](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/quickstart)

July 10, 2025

Streaming API

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#new-graphql-queries-for-wallet-trading-data)

New GraphQL Queries for Wallet Trading Data
===================================================================================================================================

![New GraphQL Queries for Wallet Trading Data](https://www.datocms-assets.com/86369/1752247757-goldrush-streaming-api-new-graphql-queries.jpg)New GraphQL queries, as part of the GoldRush Streaming API, are now available in public Beta. These queries provides real-time insights into wallet trading data and include:

*   **Get top trading wallets for token**: provides a list of wallets with the highest trading volume for a specific token over the last 30 days, along with detailed information about their holdings, transaction activity, realized and unrealized profit/loss metrics
*   **Get PnL for wallet**: provides detailed financial metrics, including unrealized and realized profit and loss (PnL), current balance, and transaction insights for each token held by a specific wallet address on a given chain.

These queries are ideal for:

*   Trading platforms that enable copy trading or following strategies of high-performing wallets.
*   Portfolio trackers and personal finance dashboards.
*   Trading bots and dashboards that highlight whale wallet activity or smart money moves.

**Note:** The GoldRush Streaming API is currently in Beta. It is stable for testing and evaluation but may undergo changes in schema or behavior as we continue to improve it. No API credits are currently charged.We welcome your feedback so please [reach out](https://goldrush.dev/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#9deee8ededf2efe9ddfef2ebfcf1f8f3e9f5ecb3fef2f0)
 to us directly to report issues or request features.[Learn more](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#july-3%2C-2025)

July 3, 2025

Mcp Server

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#goldrush-mcp-server-v0-0-3-multi-transport-support-release)

GoldRush MCP Server v0.0.3 - Multi-Transport Support Release
===================================================================================================================================================================

![GoldRush MCP Server v0.0.3 - Multi-Transport Support Release](https://www.datocms-assets.com/86369/1751673289-goldrush-mcp-multi-transport-support-release.jpg)GoldRush MCP Server is a Model Context Protocol server that enables AI applications to access blockchain and cryptocurrency data through a standardized interface. The server provides AI models with secure, structured access to blockchain data and cryptocurrency information, allowing them to answer questions and perform tasks related to digital assets, transactions, and market data.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#previous-limitations)

Previous Limitations
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Previously, users could only run the GoldRush MCP Server using STDIO transport, which limited deployment flexibility. This meant:

*   Only command-line and local integrations were possible
*   No web-based or HTTP API access
*   Limited options for authentication and security
*   Fewer deployment scenarios for production environments

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#new-capabilities)

New Capabilities
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

With this update, users can now:

*   **Deploy over HTTP**: Run the server as a web service with HTTP transport, enabling web applications and remote integrations
*   **Choose deployment method**: Select between STDIO (for local/command-line use) or HTTP (for web services) based on their needs
*   **Secure with authentication**: Use Bearer token authentication for HTTP deployments to protect access
*   **Customize configurations**: Set custom ports and configure transport settings via command-line arguments
*   **Integrate more easily**: Connect from web applications, mobile apps, or any system that can make HTTP requests

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#impact)

Impact
---------------------------------------------------------

This release significantly expands how and where GoldRush MCP Server can be deployed, making it more versatile for different use cases from local development to production web services.[Learn more](https://www.npmjs.com/package/@covalenthq/goldrush-mcp-server)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#june-4%2C-2025)

June 4, 2025

Streaming API

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#streaming-api-launch)

Streaming API Launch!
======================================================================================

![Streaming API Launch!](https://www.datocms-assets.com/86369/1750367006-goldrush-streaming-api.jpg)The GoldRush Streaming API is now available in public Beta! It provides real-time updates on blockchain events, including:

*   Token balances
*   New DEX pairs (on Uniswap V2, V3)
*   Wallet activity
*   OHLCV token and pair price data.

This API is ideal for applications that require immediate notifications or updates on blockchain activities such as:

*   Trading bots
*   Gaming
*   AI agents

The API is offered via GraphQL endpoints allowing developers to filter for specific chains, or DEXs and to start real-time subscriptions.**Note:** The GoldRush Streaming API is currently in Beta. It is stable for testing and evaluation but may undergo changes in schema or behavior as we continue to improve it. No API credits are currently charged.We welcome your feedback so please [reach out](https://goldrush.dev/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#aedddbdedec1dcdaeecdc1d8cfc2cbc0dac6df80cdc1c3)
 to us directly to report issues or request features.[Learn more](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/overview)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#may-21%2C-2025)

May 21, 2025

Foundational API

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#upgrade-to-cross-chain-address-activity-api)

Upgrade to Cross Chain Address Activity API
===================================================================================================================================

![Upgrade to Cross Chain Address Activity API](https://www.datocms-assets.com/86369/1750368404-address-activity-improvement.jpg)The Cross Chain Address Activity API has undergone a major performance improvement to significantly reduce the number of timeouts or `503` network error responses. The improvement stems from optimizing the unified query conducted over multiple shards.The Cross Chain Address Activity API does a deep crawl across all supported blockchains to identify which chains a wallet is active on along with a `last_seen_at` timestamp with one API call.[Learn more](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/cross-chain/get-address-activity)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#april-14%2C-2025)

MCP Server for Blockchain Data
=========================================================================================================

![MCP Server for Blockchain Data](https://www.datocms-assets.com/86369/1750367375-goldrush-mcp-banner.jpg)The GoldRush MCP Server exposes the GoldRush APIs as MCP resources and tools, enabling LLMs to interact with extensive, structured, multichain data.Developers and product teams can leverage the GoldRush MCP server to power AI-driven use-cases such as:

*   Real-time blockchain analytics and insights directly within conversational AI and assistants.
*   Enhanced risk assessment and compliance tools powered by AI with live on-chain data feeds.
*   Dynamic NFT and DeFi marketplaces utilizing AI-driven discovery and recommendation engines based on real-time blockchain activity.
*   AI Agents: Enable autonomous AI agents to fetch, analyze, and act upon blockchain data in real-time, powering automated trading strategies, monitoring, and governance mechanisms.

[Learn more](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-mcp-server)

Enhanced Token Spam Lists
===============================================================================================

![Enhanced Token Spam Lists](https://www.datocms-assets.com/86369/1743204211-spam-token-list-expansion.jpg)With the release of the [Enhanced Spam Lists](https://goldrush.dev/docs/resources/enhanced-spam-lists)
 for ERC20 tokens and NFTs across all [Foundational Chains](https://goldrush.dev/chains/)
, the following GoldRush APIs are now seamlessly updated to leverage these lists:

*   [Get token balances for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/balances/get-token-balances-for-address)
     using the `no-spam` query parameter.
*   [Get historical token balances for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address)
     using the `no-spam` query parameter.
*   [Get NFTs for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/nft/get-nfts-for-address)
     using the `no-spam` query parameter.

In addition, any of the API responses with the `is_spam` field will incorporate the Enhanced Spam Lists.[Learn more](https://goldrush.dev/docs/resources/enhanced-spam-lists)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#february-20%2C-2025)

February 20, 2025

Foundational API

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#update-to-token-holders-api)

Update to Token Holders API
===================================================================================================

![Update to Token Holders API](https://www.datocms-assets.com/86369/1741047446-token-holders-api-update-feb2025.jpg)The following changes were made to the [Token Holders API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/balances/get-token-holders-as-of-any-block-height-v2)
:

*   When no `block-height` is specified, the response is from the latest token holder snapshot that is updated every 30 minutes. This results in a fast response time.
*   To fetch the current token holders list without using the snapshot, set `no-snapshot=true`. This bypasses the cache and is dynamically calculated at request time.

The snapshot exists for the top 100 tokens on each [Foundational Chain](https://goldrush.dev/chains/)
 as listed on [CoinGecko](https://www.coingecko.com/en/categories/ethereum-ecosystem)
.This modification is to help address the two unique use cases for this API:

1.  Displaying a list of token holders on leaderboards to provide guidance on a token’s distribution. This list does not generally need to be accurate to the minute.
2.  Token holder lists for reward distributions and token gating. This is generally an accurate token list generated at a specific point in time.

[Learn more](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/balances/get-token-holders-as-of-any-block-height-v2)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#february-20%2C-2025-2)

February 1, 2025

General

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#update-to-the-goldrush-professional-tier-and-pricing-change)

Update to the GoldRush Professional Tier and Pricing Change
===================================================================================================================================================================

There are some significant updates to our pricing structure, which were announced in late August, 2024, that are now in effect as of February 1, 2025.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#what-has-changed)

What has Changed?

**Our new Professional Tier has replaced the Premium Tier.**

*   Professional Tier: $250 per month for 300,000 API credits, with overages at 0.00077 per credit.
*   Existing Premium Tier users: You need to transition to the Professional Tier to ensure you continue to receive the same high-quality performance and features.

If you prefer the existing Premium Tier pricing, you can sign up through [one of our channel partners](https://goldrush.dev/pricing/)
 where the Premium Tier is available at $50/month for 50,000 credits.**Our Free Tier has ended and replaced with the Free Trial.**

*   Existing grandfathered Free Tier users who signed up before the 14-day Free Trial was implemented will now need to upgrade to a paid tier effective February 1, 2025.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#why-the-changes)

Why the Changes?

We are making these updates to:

*   Ensure consistent pricing for our API across various marketplaces.
*   Provide better and more responsive support.
*   Maintain and enhance the quality of our services.

For any questions or assistance, please contact us at [\[email protected\]](https://goldrush.dev/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#bdcec8cdcdd2cfc9fdded2cbdcd1d8d3c9d5cc93ded2d0)
.[Learn more](https://goldrush.dev/pricing/)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#january-29%2C-2025)

January 29, 2025

Foundational API

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#new-dex-pool-spot-prices-api)

New DEX pool spot prices API
=====================================================================================================

![New DEX pool spot prices API](https://www.datocms-assets.com/86369/1743209907-dex-pool-spot-prices.jpg)Given the meme coin trading hype, GoldRush has released a new DEX pool spot prices API that supports pools on Uniswap V2, V3 and their forks on all [Foundational Chains](https://goldrush.dev/chains)
.The API takes in the `contractAddress` of the pool and returns the following key fields:

*   `token_0_price` - Price of `token_0` in units of `token_1`.
*   `token_0_price_24` - Price of `token_0` in units of `token_1` as of 24 hours ago.
*   `token_0_price_quote` - Price of `token_0` in the selected quote currency (defaults to `USD`)
*   Similar values for `token_1_xx` making up the pool pair.

This API leverages the onchain sync event to get the spot prices.[Learn more](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/utility/get-pool-spot-prices)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#december-12%2C-2024)

December 12, 2024

Foundational API

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#tracing-enhancements-supported-on-ethereum)

Tracing Enhancements Supported on Ethereum
=================================================================================================================================

![Tracing Enhancements Supported on Ethereum](https://www.datocms-assets.com/86369/1741045831-tracing-enhancements-on-ethereum.jpg)Introducing the following tracing enhancements to our [Multichain & Multiaddress Transactions API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/cross-chain/get-allchains-transactions)
 and [Get a Transaction](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/transactions/get-a-transaction)
 for `ethereum-mainnet`:

*   Internal Transactions
*   State Changes
*   Input Data

Use the following query params:

*   `with-internal` - includes internal transfers/transactions in the chain’s native token.
*   `with-state` - includes all transaction state changes with before and after values
*   `with-input-data` - includes the transaction’s input data, currently just the Method ID.

[Learn more](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/cross-chain/get-allchains-balances)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#december-10%2C-2024)

December 10, 2024

Foundational API

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#new-multichain-balances-api)

New Multichain Balances API
===================================================================================================

![New Multichain Balances API](https://www.datocms-assets.com/86369/1741044671-multichain-balances_v2.jpg)Introducing the new GoldRush Multichain Balances API where you can fetch paginated spot & historical native and token balances for a single address on up to 10 EVM chains with one API call.Some key points to note:

*   The pagination method used for this API are **cursors** . Note the response includes the following cursor specific fields:
    *   `cursor_before` - fetch token balances before a certain point in the response.
    *   The values of these fields can be passed as query params to scroll through the token balances using `before={cursor_before}`.
*   If `cursor_before=null` , you have reached the first page of the token balances list.
*   ALL supported chains can be passed in the `chains=` query param (both chain names and ID’s are supported) up to a maximum of 10 chains.
*   When no chains are specified, the API defaults to use the [Foundational Chains](https://goldrush.dev/chains/)
    .
*   ERC20 token spam filtering is currently not supported but will be added. In the response, `is_spam` will always default to `false`.
*   When the `cutoff-timestamp` query param is passed, the balance snapshot will be from the nearest block _before_ the specified cutoff time.

[Learn more](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/cross-chain/get-allchains-balances)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#november-18%2C-2024)

November 18, 2024

General

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#goldrush-changes-phase-1:-chain-classification-&-prioritization)

GoldRush Changes Phase 1: Chain Classification & Prioritization
===========================================================================================================================================================================

GoldRush is reorganizing its support for various chains by grouping them into four distinct categories:**Foundational Chains:** These are the top EVM-compatible chains that have achieved wide adoption. For these chains, GoldRush guarantees product parity across its entire suite of features. This includes tracing enhancements, historical token balances, token holders, and cached NFT assets. In addition, we’ll provide ecosystem support in the form of API credits, hackathon bounties, workshops, guides, and co-marketing activities.**Frontier Chains:** These chains, both EVM and non-EVM compatible, represent the cutting edge of blockchain innovation. While not all product features will be available for Frontier Chains, GoldRush will continue to offer its core APIs at an enterprise level, along with ecosystem support.**Community Chains:** These chains include those with passionate builder communities and will will offer core APIs including balances, transactions, and decoded log events.**Archived Chains:** No live data will be available for archived chains. Only historical data will continue to be provided for a brief period of time.[Learn more](https://goldrush.dev/chains/)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#november-18%2C-2024-2)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#new-multichain-&-multiaddress-transactions-api)

New Multichain & Multiaddress Transactions API
=========================================================================================================================================

![New Multichain & Multiaddress Transactions API](https://www.datocms-assets.com/86369/1732748430-multichain-multiaddress-transactions.jpg)Introducing the new GoldRush Multichain & Multiaddress Transactions API where you can fetch transactions for up to 10 EVM addresses across 10 EVM chains with one API call.Some key points to note:

*   The pagination method used for this API are **cursors** . Note the response includes the following cursor specific fields:
    *   `cursor_before`
    *   `cursor_after` The values of these fields can be passed as query params to scroll through the transactions using `before={cursor_before}` or `after={cursor_after}`
*   If `cursor_before=null` , you’ve reached the first page of the descending transaction list
*   Cursors are linked to the list of chains that transactions are fetched from. If, for example, you obtain a `cursor_before` value when querying `chains=1,56` and then try to use that value with `chains=1,137` , you will get an error.
*   ALL supported chains can be passed in the `chains=` query param (both chain names and ID’s are supported) up to a maximum of 10 chains.
*   When no chains are specified, the API defaults to use the [Foundational Chains](https://goldrush.dev/chains/)
    .

[Learn more](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/cross-chain/get-allchains-transactions)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#october-16%2C-2024)

No live data will be available for these chains.See the current list of Archived Chains [here](https://goldrush.dev/chains)
.In general, GoldRush is reorganizing its prioritization and support for various chains with more on this to be announced soon.[Learn more](https://goldrush.dev/chains/)

Introducing the Customizable Block Explorer Template
=====================================================================================================================================================

![Introducing the Customizable Block Explorer Template](https://www.datocms-assets.com/86369/1732742509-goldrush-block-explorer-template.jpg)Leveraging the GoldRush UI Kit, the customizable [GoldRush Block Explorer template](https://goldrush-block-explorer.vercel.app/)
works seamlessly across all supported chains and is designed to make onchain verification and exploration easier than ever.Some of the key features are:

*   Real-time Block Explorer: Provides up-to-date information on blockchain transactions, blocks, and account balances in real time, giving users the latest data.
*   Ready-to-use customizable template: Jumpstart your dApp journey with a beautifully designed UI that’s both intuitive and engaging.
*   Cross Chain Support: Supports 100+ chains, providing a unified explorer for all your needs.
*   Comprehensive Data Filtering: Search and filter through blockchain data with options to refine by transaction type, block height, or account, making it ideal for both casual users and developers.
*   UI Template: The GoldRush Block Explorer can be customized with different colors and modes per deployment.

[Learn more](https://github.com/covalenthq/goldrush-block-explorer-ui)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#september-1%2C-2024)

September 1, 2024

General

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#introducing-the-goldrush-professional-tier-and-pricing-change)

Introducing the GoldRush Professional Tier and Pricing Change
=======================================================================================================================================================================

There are some significant updates to our pricing structure, effective September 1, 2024.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#what%E2%80%99s-changing)

What’s Changing?

**Our new Professional Tier will replace the Premium Tier.**

*   Professional Tier: $250 per month for 300,000 API credits, with overages at 0.00077 per credit.
*   Existing Premium Tier users: You can continue with your current plan until February 1, 2025. You will then need to transition to the Professional Tier to ensure you continue to receive the same high-quality performance and features.

If you prefer the existing Premium Tier pricing, you can sign up through [one of our channel partners](https://goldrush.dev/pricing/)
 where the Premium Tier is available at $50/month for 50,000 credits.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#why-the-changes-2)

Why the Changes?

We are making these updates to:

*   Ensure consistent pricing for our API across various marketplaces.
*   Provide better and more responsive support.
*   Maintain and enhance the quality of our services.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#what%E2%80%99s-next)

What’s Next?

The new Professional Tier will offer the same performance and features you’ve come to expect from our Premium Tier. We’ll provide more details soon, and we’re here to support you during this transition. For any questions or assistance, please contact us at [\[email protected\]](https://goldrush.dev/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#45363035352a373105262a332429202b312d346b262a28)
.[Learn more](https://goldrush.dev/pricing/)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#july-31%2C-2024)

July 31, 2024

API

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/changelog#new-non-breaking-import-statement-for-goldrush-sdks)

New (Non-Breaking) Import Statement for GoldRush SDKs
=====================================================================================================================================================

![New (Non-Breaking) Import Statement for GoldRush SDKs](https://www.datocms-assets.com/86369/1722467559-goldrush-sdk.jpg)Following the rebrand of Covalent’s data products to “GoldRush”, the following import statement is now supported through the SDKs: `import { GoldRushClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";`This is a non-breaking change, so projects using `import { CovalentClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";` will be unaffected.[Learn more](https://goldrush.dev/docs/unified-api/quickstart/typescript-sdk/)

Use Cases
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![1748642802-streaming-api-products-ohlcv](https://www.datocms-assets.com/86369/1748642802-streaming-api-products-ohlcv.png)

Trading Bots
------------

Power your bots with new pairs, pair liquidity changes, OHLCV pricing data, and wallet activity to copy trade.

![1748642719-streaming-api-products-gamefi](https://www.datocms-assets.com/86369/1748642719-streaming-api-products-gamefi.png)

Gaming
------

Stream inventory balances and onchain game state right into your game engine with no lag or polling.

![1748642703-streaming-api-products-ai](https://www.datocms-assets.com/86369/1748642703-streaming-api-products-ai.png)

AI Agents
---------

Power your AI Agents with streaming wallet information to build novel co-pilot apps.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/overview#available-streams)

Available Streams
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The GoldRush Streaming API offers the following streams:

*   [**OHLCV Tokens Stream**](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-tokens-stream)
    : Continuous price data feed providing Open, High, Low, Close, Volume values for one or many tokens at configurable intervals. Commonly used to execute trading strategies like take-profit, stop-loss and others.
*   [**OHLCV Pairs Stream**](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-pairs-stream)
    : Continuous price data feed providing Open, High, Low, Close, Volume values for one or many token pairs at configurable intervals. Commonly used to execute trading strategies like take-profit, stop-loss and others.
*   [**New DEX Pairs Stream**](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/new-dex-pairs-stream)
    : Real-time updates on new pairs, pair liquidity changes, and other pair-related events across supported DEXes. Commonly used to build liquidity sniping bots.
*   [**Update Pairs Stream**](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/update-pairs)
    : Real-time price, liquidity, volume, and market cap updates for tracked token pairs. Commonly used to monitor portfolio exposure or trigger alerting workflows.
*   [**Wallet Activity Stream**](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/wallet-activity-stream)
    : Live tracking of wallet transactions, token transfers, and interactions with smart contracts. Commonly used to build copy trading bots.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/overview#supported-chains-&-dexes)

Supported Chains & DEXes
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Chain | Supported DEXes |
| --- | --- |
| `BASE_MAINNET` | *   `VIRTUALS_V2`<br>*   `CLANKER`<br>*   `UNISWAP_V2`<br>*   `UNISWAP_V3` |
| `SOLANA_MAINNET` | *   `RAYDIUM_AMM`<br>*   `RAYDIUM_CPMM`<br>*   `PUMP_FUN`<br>*   `PUMP_FUN_AMM`<br>*   `MOONSHOT`<br>*   `RAYDIUM_LAUNCH_LAB`<br>*   `METEORA_DAMM`<br>*   `METEORA_DLMM`<br>*   `METEORA_DBC` |
| `ETH_MAINNET` | *   `UNISWAP_V2`<br>*   `UNISWAP_V3` |
| `BSC_MAINNET` | *   `PANCAKESWAP_V2`<br>*   `PANCAKESWAP_V3` |
| `SONIC_MAINNET` | *   `SHADOW_V2`<br>*   `SHADOW_V3` |
| `MONAD_MAINNET` | *   `OCTOSWAP_V2`<br>*   `OCTOSWAP_V3` |

Overview
-------------------------------------------------------------------

GoldRush offers support for **50** blockchain networks with the most comprehensive Blockchain Data API suite for developers, analysts, and enterprises. Whether you’re building a DeFi dashboard, a wallet, a trading bot, an AI agent or a compliance platform, our Blockchain Data APIs provide fast, accurate, and developer-friendly access to the essential onchain data you need.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/quickstart#introduction)

Introduction
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This quickstart guide walks through using the [GoldRush TypeScript SDK](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/goldrush-sdks)
 to quickly build with multichain data leveraging the powerful GoldRush APIs.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/quickstart#prerequisites)

Prerequisites
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Using any of the GoldRush developer tools requires an API key.[Get Started\
-----------\
\
Sign up for a free API key to get started with GoldRush.](https://goldrush.dev/platform/auth/register/)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/quickstart#supported-chains)

Supported Chains
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

GoldRush can be used with any of the supported chains. See the full list, including chain categorization, at [Supported Chains](https://goldrush.dev/chains/)
.

Some data enrichments such as internal transactions and historical balance fetches are only available for Foundational Chains.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/quickstart#using-the-goldrush-typescript-sdk)

Using the GoldRush TypeScript SDK
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The GoldRush TypeScript SDK is the fastest way to integrate the GoldRush APIs for working with blockchain data. The SDK works with all supported chains including Mainnets and Testnets.

This SDK requires NodeJS v18 or above.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/quickstart#step-1-install-the-sdk)

Step 1. Install the SDK

npm

yarn

Copy

Ask AI

    npm install @covalenthq/client-sdk
    

See the package on [npmjs](https://www.npmjs.com/package/@covalenthq/client-sdk)
 for more details.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/quickstart#step-2-import-the-client)

Step 2. Import the Client

The `GoldRushClient` class provides typesafe, easy-to-use helper functions and classes to use the GoldRush APIs.

Copy

Ask AI

    import { GoldRushClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/quickstart#step-3-initialize-the-client)

Step 3. Initialize the Client

Copy

Ask AI

    import { GoldRushClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    const ApiServices = async () => {
        const client = new GoldRushClient("YOUR_API_KEY"); 
    };
    

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/quickstart#step-4-invoke-the-service)

Step 4. Invoke the Service

In this quickstart, we use the `BalanceService` and `getTokenBalancesForWalletAddress()` function to fetch all token balances held by an address. This function takes a chain name and wallet address as required arguments.

ENS resolution is supported for `eth-mainnet`.

Copy

Ask AI

    import { GoldRushClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    const ApiServices = async () => {
        // Replace with your GoldRush API key
        const client = new GoldRushClient("YOUR_API_KEY"); 
        const response = await client.BalanceService.getTokenBalancesForWalletAddress("eth-mainnet", "demo.eth"); 
        
        if (!response.error) {
            console.log(response.data);
        } else {
            console.log(response.error_message);
        }
    };
    
    ApiServices();
    

Example response:

Copy

Ask AI

    {
        "address": "0xfc43f5f9dd45258b3aff31bdbe6561d97e8b71de",
        "chain_id": 1,
        "chain_name": "eth-mainnet",

        "updated_at": "2024-11-05T22:18:41.522Z",

# Authentication - GoldRush API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/authentication#content-area)

[GoldRush API Documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=97917fde1507b0c14e79b83959fe1160)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=5bd4f921dcc81186bf369e7b33ec5734)](https://goldrush.dev/docs)

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

GoldRush Foundational API

Authentication

[Overview](https://goldrush.dev/docs/overview)
[Foundational API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/overview)
[Streaming API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/overview)
[Chains](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/overview)

On this page

*   [Why is Authentication Required?](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/authentication#why-is-authentication-required)
    
*   [1\. Obtaining a GoldRush API Key](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/authentication#1-obtaining-a-goldrush-api-key)
    
*   [2\. Supplying the API Key](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/authentication#2-supplying-the-api-key)
    
*   [Using SDKs (Recommended)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/authentication#using-sdks-recommended)
    
*   [Direct API Calls](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/authentication#direct-api-calls)
    
*   [Error Handling](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/authentication#error-handling)
    
*   [Frequently Asked Questions (FAQ)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/authentication#frequently-asked-questions-faq)
    

This document provides a comprehensive overview of the authentication process for the Foundational API. All APIs are protected and require a valid GoldRush API key to access. This guide covers how to obtain and use an API key, with examples for both our SDKs and direct REST API calls.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/authentication#why-is-authentication-required)

Why is Authentication Required?
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Authentication is essential to ensure that only authorized users can access the Foundational API. It allows us to manage access, track usage for billing, and ensure the security and stability of our services.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/authentication#1-obtaining-a-goldrush-api-key)

1\. Obtaining a GoldRush API Key
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To begin, register for an API key at the [GoldRush Platform](https://goldrush.dev/platform/auth/register/)
. This key will be required for all requests to the Foundational API.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/authentication#2-supplying-the-api-key)

2\. Supplying the API Key
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Foundational API offers flexible and powerful ways to access blockchain data. You can use one of our GoldRush SDKs for a streamlined experience, or make direct HTTP requests to the various REST APIs.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/authentication#using-sdks-recommended)

Using SDKs (Recommended)

For easier integration and to take advantage of built-in features like automatic retries and rate limit handling, we recommend using the TypeScript Client SDK.

*   TypeScript
    

Initialize the client with your API key:

Copy

Ask AI

    import { GoldRushClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    const ApiServices = async () => {
        const client = new GoldRushClient("YOUR_API_KEY_HERE"); // Replace with your GoldRush API key
        const resp = await client.BalanceService.getTokenBalancesForWalletAddress({
            chainName: "eth-mainnet",
            walletAddress: "vitalik.eth"
        });
        
        if (!resp.error) {
            console.log(resp.data);
        } else {
            console.log(resp.error_message);
        }
    };
    
    ApiServices();
    

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/authentication#direct-api-calls)

Direct API Calls

You can also authenticate by including your API key in direct HTTP requests.

Basic Authentication

Provide your API key as the Basic Auth username. You do not need to provide a password. The trailing colon (`:`) prevents `curl` from prompting for a password.

Copy

Ask AI

    curl -X GET https://api.covalenthq.com/v1/eth-mainnet/address/demo.eth/balances_v2/ \
         -u YOUR_API_KEY_HERE: \
         -H 'Content-Type: application/json'
Bearer Token

Provide your API key in an `Authorization` header with the `Bearer` scheme.

Copy

Ask AI

    curl -X GET https://api.covalenthq.com/v1/eth-mainnet/address/demo.eth/balances_v2/ \
         -H 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_API_KEY_HERE'
Query Parameter

Include your API key as the `key` query parameter in the request URL.

Copy

Ask AI

    curl -X GET "https://api.covalenthq.com/v1/eth-mainnet/address/demo.eth/balances_v2/?key=YOUR_API_KEY_HERE"

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/authentication#error-handling)

Error Handling
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If an authentication-related error occurs, the API will return a `4XX` HTTP status code and a JSON body with details.

| Code | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `401 - Unauthorized` | No valid API key was provided, or the key is incorrect. |
| `402 - Payment Required` | The account has consumed its allocated API credits. |
| `429 - Too Many Requests` | You are being rate-limited. |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/authentication#frequently-asked-questions-faq)

Frequently Asked Questions (FAQ)
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Which authentication method should I use?**
    *   We strongly recommend using our [SDKs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/authentication#using-sdks-recommended)
         for the best developer experience. If you must make direct API calls, **Basic Authentication** is preferred over other methods for its security. Placing API keys in URLs (query parameter) is generally discouraged.
*   **Where can I find my API Key?**
    *   You can find your API key on the [GoldRush Platform](https://goldrush.dev/platform/auth/register/)
         after signing up or logging in.
*   **Are the API keys the same for the different GoldRush products?**
    *   Yes, the same API key is used to authenticate with all GoldRush products.

[Quickstart](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/quickstart)
[Get activity across all chains for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-address-activity)

⌘I

# Enhanced Bitcoin Support - GoldRush API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://goldrush.dev/docs/resources/enhanced-bitcoin-support#content-area)

[GoldRush API Documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=97917fde1507b0c14e79b83959fe1160)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=5bd4f921dcc81186bf369e7b33ec5734)](https://goldrush.dev/docs)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Resources

Enhanced Bitcoin Support

[Overview](https://goldrush.dev/docs/overview)
[Foundational API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/overview)
[Streaming API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/overview)
[Chains](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/overview)

On this page

*   [Key Concepts](https://goldrush.dev/docs/resources/enhanced-bitcoin-support#key-concepts)
    
*   [Capabilities](https://goldrush.dev/docs/resources/enhanced-bitcoin-support#capabilities)
    
*   [API endpoints](https://goldrush.dev/docs/resources/enhanced-bitcoin-support#api-endpoints)
    

GoldRush offers production-grade Bitcoin data for wallets, tax tools, explorers, and analytics. We operate dedicated Bitcoin node infrastructure and index the chain from the genesis block to ensure complete, accurate balance and transaction history.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/resources/enhanced-bitcoin-support#key-concepts)

Key Concepts

*   **Hierarchical Deterministic (HD) Wallet** refers to a wallet that generates all of its keys and addresses from a single source (e.g. a seed phrase). These keys and addresses can be organized into a tree (hierarchial) and are always generated the same way (deterministic).
*   **Extended public keys** (e.g., `xpub...`, `ypub...`, `zpub...`) are HD address-level public keys used to derive many child receive addresses.
*   **Non-HD addresses or child addresses** follow different standards:
    *   **BIP44 Legacy, P2PKH**: addresses typically start with `1`, derived path `m/44'/0'/...`
    *   **BIP49 Nested SegWit, P2SH-P2WPKH**: addresses typically start with `3`, derived path `m/49'/0'/...`
    *   **BIP84 Native SegWit, P2WPKH/bech32**: addresses typically start with `bc1`, derived path `m/84'/0'/...`
    *   **BIP86 Taproot, P2TR**: addresses typically start with `bc1p`, derived path `m/86'/0'/...`

For an excellent resource to understand HD wallets and derivation paths, see: [Learn Me A Bitcoin - HD Wallets](https://learnmeabitcoin.com/technical/keys/hd-wallets/)

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/resources/enhanced-bitcoin-support#capabilities)

Capabilities

*   **Full-chain ingestion**: Dedicated node and indexers ingest all Bitcoin transactions from genesis for complete historical coverage.
*   **Extensive HD wallet derivation scans (gap limit 20)**: We continue to derive child addresses until encountering 20 consecutive child addresses with zero balance and no transaction history.
*   **Support multiple child address formats**: Includes BIP44 Legacy, BIP49 Nested SegWit, BIP84 Native SegWit.
*   **Spot and historical balances for non-HD/child addresses**: Includes current and historical **fiat price** conversions.
*   **Spot balances for derived child addresses from HD wallet addresses (xpub/ypub/zpub)**: Includes spot balances, fiat prices and 24hr deltas.
*   **Historical transactions for non-HD addresses**: Retrieve time-ordered transactions for a Bitcoin address for statements, tax, and activity feed workflows.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/resources/enhanced-bitcoin-support#api-endpoints)

API endpoints

*   [Get Bitcoin balances for HD address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balances-for-hd-address)
    
*   [Get Bitcoin balance for non-HD address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balance-for-address)
    
*   [Get historical Bitcoin balance for non-HD address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-bitcoin-balance-for-address)
    
*   [Get transactions for Bitcoin non-HD address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-transactions-for-bitcoin-address)
    

[Get resolved address for registered address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-resolved-address-for-registered-address)
[NFT Supported Formats](https://goldrush.dev/docs/resources/nft-supported-formats)

⌘I

# NFT Supported Formats - GoldRush API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://goldrush.dev/docs/resources/nft-supported-formats#content-area)

[GoldRush API Documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=97917fde1507b0c14e79b83959fe1160)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=5bd4f921dcc81186bf369e7b33ec5734)](https://goldrush.dev/docs)

Resources

NFT Supported Formats

[Overview](https://goldrush.dev/docs/overview)
[Foundational API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/overview)
[Streaming API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/overview)
[Chains](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/overview)

On this page

*   [Decoding base64 thumbhash](https://goldrush.dev/docs/resources/nft-supported-formats#decoding-base64-thumbhash)
    

The GoldRush API supports the following NFT formats: **Images:**

*   `image/png`
*   `image/jpeg`
*   `image/gif`
*   `image/svg+xml`
*   `image/webp`
*   `image/bmp`
*   `image/tiff`
*   `image/vnd.adobe.photoshop`
*   `image/avif`
*   `image/heic`
*   `image/jp2`
*   `image/heif`
*   `image/x-canon-cr2`

**Videos:**

Images are rendered as thumbnails of the first frame of the video.

*   `video/mp4`
*   `video/quicktime`
*   `video/x-m4v`
*   `video/3gpp`
*   `video/webm`
*   `video/x-matroska`
*   `video/x-ms-wmv`
*   `video/mpeg`
*   `video/x-flv`
*   `video/x-msvideo`

**Audio:**

Images are rendered as thumbnails of an audio waveform.

*   `audio/mp4`
*   `audio/mpeg`
*   `audio/vnd.wave`
*   `audio/vorbis`
*   `audio/x-flac`
*   `audio/x-m4a`
*   `audio/x-wav`

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/resources/nft-supported-formats#decoding-base64-thumbhash)

Decoding base64 thumbhash
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Developers can use the [thumbhash npm package](https://www.npmjs.com/package/thumbhash)
 to decode the hash into a data url:

Copy

Ask AI

    ThumbHash.thumbHashToDataURL(new Uint8Array(atob("ewgGDwLG3DVomId/dkSKhmlsubILoKgC").split('').map(x => x.charCodeAt(0))))
    

This results in a data url(copy paste in chrome to see the blurred version of the asset image created using thumbhash):

Copy

Ask AI

# Enhanced Spam Lists - GoldRush API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://goldrush.dev/docs/resources/enhanced-spam-lists#content-area)

[GoldRush API Documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=97917fde1507b0c14e79b83959fe1160)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=5bd4f921dcc81186bf369e7b33ec5734)](https://goldrush.dev/docs)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Resources

Enhanced Spam Lists

[Overview](https://goldrush.dev/docs/overview)
[Foundational API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/overview)
[Streaming API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/overview)
[Chains](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/overview)

On this page

*   [Step 1. Install the Package](https://goldrush.dev/docs/resources/enhanced-spam-lists#step-1-install-the-package)
    
*   [Step 2. Use Cases](https://goldrush.dev/docs/resources/enhanced-spam-lists#step-2-use-cases)
    

The GoldRush Enhanced Spam Lists are a public good designed to restore trust and transparency in the Web3 ecosystem by helping developers, explorers, wallets, and indexers protect their users from scam tokens and malicious contracts. The Enhanced Spam Lists can be accessed as an [npm package](https://www.npmjs.com/package/@covalenthq/goldrush-enhanced-spam-lists)
.

This package requires Node.js v18 or above.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/resources/enhanced-spam-lists#step-1-install-the-package)

Step 1. Install the Package

You can install the package using npm, yarn or pnpm:

npm

yarn

pnpm

Copy

Ask AI

    npm install @covalenthq/goldrush-enhanced-spam-lists
    

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/resources/enhanced-spam-lists#step-2-use-cases)

Step 2. Use Cases

1

Verify if an ERC20 token is spam on a given network

Copy

Ask AI

    import {
        Networks,
        isERC20Spam,
    } from "@covalenthq/goldrush-enhanced-spam-lists";
    
    // With default options
    const isSpam = await isERC20Spam("0xTokenAddress", Networks.ETHEREUM_MAINNET);
    console.log(isSpam);
    

2

For a potential spam check for an ERC20 token, Confidence.MAYBE can be used

Copy

Ask AI

    import {
        Confidence,
        Networks,
        isERC20Spam,
    } from "@covalenthq/goldrush-enhanced-spam-lists";
    
    const isPotentialSpam = await isERC20Spam(
        "0xTokenAddress",
        Networks.POLYGON_MAINNET,
        Confidence.MAYBE
    );
    console.log(isPotentialSpam);
    

3

Verify if an NFT token is spam on a given network

Copy

Ask AI

    import {
            Networks,
            isNFTSpam,
    } from "@covalenthq/goldrush-enhanced-spam-lists";
    
    const isNftSpam = await isNFTSpam("0xNftAddress", Networks.BSC_MAINNET);
    console.log(isNftSpam);
    

4

Control caching behavior

Copy

Ask AI

    import {
        Networks,
        Confidence,
        isERC20Spam,
        clearCache,
    } from "@covalenthq/goldrush-enhanced-spam-lists";
    
    // With caching enabled (default)
    const withCache = await isERC20Spam(
        "0xTokenAddress",
        Networks.ETHEREUM_MAINNET,
        Confidence.YES,
        true // Enable caching (default)
    );
    
    // Without caching (always fetches fresh data)
    const withoutCache = await isERC20Spam(
        "0xTokenAddress",
        Networks.ETHEREUM_MAINNET,
        Confidence.YES,
        false // Disable caching
    );
    
    // Clear memory and disk cache if needed
    clearCache();
    

5

For more control, you can get the full lists:

Copy

Ask AI

    import {
        getERC20List,
        getNFTList,
        Confidence,
        Networks,
    } from "@covalenthq/goldrush-enhanced-spam-lists";
    
    // Get ERC20 spam list with default caching
    const ethSpamTokens = await getERC20List(Networks.ETHEREUM_MAINNET, Confidence.YES);
    
    // Get NFT spam list with caching disabled
    const bscSpamNfts = await getNFTList(Networks.BSC_MAINNET, false);
    

6

Get the specific spam score for a given contract

Copy

Ask AI

    import {
        getERC20List,
        getSpamScore,
        Networks,
        Confidence,
    } from "@covalenthq/goldrush-enhanced-spam-lists";
    
    const ethSpamTokens = await getERC20List(
    Networks.ETHEREUM_MAINNET,
    Confidence.YES
    );
    const score = getSpamScore(ethSpamTokens[0]);
    console.log(score); // Returns the spam score as a string
    

[NFT Supported Formats](https://goldrush.dev/docs/resources/nft-supported-formats)

Overview
--------------------------------------------------------------------

GoldRush offers the most comprehensive ADI Chain Data API suite for developers, analysts, and enterprises. Whether you’re building a DeFi dashboard, a wallet, a trading bot, an AI agent or a compliance platform, our ADI Chain Data APIs provide fast, accurate, and developer-friendly access to the essential onchain data you need.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/adi-chain#supported-apis)

Supported APIs

[Foundational API\
----------------\
\
Access structured historical blockchain data across 100+ chains using REST APIs. Get token balances, transaction histories, decoded event logs, NFT assets, token holders and more.  \
  \
**Use cases: Wallets, portfolio trackers, crypto accounting & tax tools, and DeFi dashboards.**\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/adi-chain#mainnet)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/adi-chain#api-usage)

API Usage
----------------------------------------------------------------------

To use this blockchain network in GoldRush API calls, use:

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/adi-chain#chain-name)

Chain Name

*   `adi-mainnet` (mainnet)
*   `adi-testnet` (testnet)

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/adi-chain#example-api-calls)

Example API Calls

Chain Name (Mainnet)

Chain Name (ADI Testnet)

Copy

Ask AI

    curl -X GET "https://api.covalenthq.com/v1/adi-mainnet/address/0xd8dA6BF26964aF9D7eEd9e03E53415D37aA96045/balances_v2/?key=API_KEY"
    

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/adi-chain#sdk-usage)

SDK Usage

TypeScript SDK (Mainnet)

TypeScript SDK (ADI Testnet)

Copy

Ask AI

    import { GoldRushClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    const client = new GoldRushClient("API_KEY");
    const resp = await client.BalanceService.getTokenBalancesForWalletAddress({
        chainName: "adi-mainnet",
        walletAddress: "0xd8dA6BF26964aF9D7eEd9e03E53415D37aA96045"
    });

Overview
--------------------------------------------------------------

GoldRush offers the most comprehensive Arc Testnet Data API suite for developers, analysts, and enterprises. Whether you’re building a DeFi dashboard, a wallet, a trading bot, an AI agent or a compliance platform, our Arc Testnet Data APIs provide fast, accurate, and developer-friendly access to the essential onchain data you need.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/arc#supported-apis)

Supported APIs

[Foundational API\
----------------\
\

  \
**Use cases: Wallets, portfolio trackers, crypto accounting & tax tools, and DeFi dashboards.**\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api)

GoldRush Streaming API

Quickstart

[Overview](https://goldrush.dev/docs/overview)
[Foundational API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/overview)
[Streaming API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/overview)
[Chains](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/overview)

On this page

*   [Prerequisites](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/quickstart#prerequisites)
    
*   [Connection](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/quickstart#connection)
