[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/quickstart#prerequisites)

Prerequisites
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Using any of the GoldRush developer tools requires an API key.[Get Started\
-----------\
\
Sign up for a free API key to get started with GoldRush.](https://goldrush.dev/platform/auth/register/)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/quickstart#connection)

Connection
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Streaming API supports GraphQL subscriptions over WebSocket, using the [GraphQL over WebSocket](https://github.com/enisdenjo/graphql-ws/blob/master/PROTOCOL.md)
 protocol. The recommended approach is to use the official [TypeScript Client SDK](https://www.npmjs.com/package/@covalenthq/client-sdk)
 which supports the Streaming API and manages all WebSocket connections.

npm

yarn

Copy

Ask AI

    npm install @covalenthq/client-sdk
    

You can also use a GraphQL over WebSocket protocol npm package like [`graphql-ws`](https://www.npmjs.com/package/graphql-ws)
.

If you’re not using the `graphql-ws` package, you must set the WebSocket protocol header:`"Sec-WebSocket-Protocol" : "graphql-transport-ws"`This header is required for the server to properly recognize and handle your GraphQL subscription requests.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/quickstart#ohlcv-token-stream-code-samples)

OHLCV Token Stream Code Samples
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The following examples show how to connect and subscribe to the OHLCV Token stream using your preferred language or tool. Each sample connects to the WebSocket endpoint, authenticates with your API key, and streams real-time OHLCV updates for a token on Base Mainnet.

GoldRush SDK

TypeScript (graphql-ws)

Python

Terminal (websocat)

Copy

Ask AI

    import {
      GoldRushClient,
      StreamingChain,
      StreamingInterval,
      StreamingTimeframe
    } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    const client = new GoldRushClient(
      "<GOLDRUSH_API_KEY>",
      {},
      {
        onConnecting: () => console.log("Connecting to streaming service..."),
        onOpened: () => console.log("Connected to streaming service!"),
        onClosed: () => console.log("Disconnected from streaming service"),
        onError: (error) => console.error("Streaming error:", error),
      }
    );
    
    client.StreamingService.subscribeToOHLCVTokens(
      {
        chain_name: StreamingChain.BASE_MAINNET,
        token_addresses: ["0x0b3e328455c4059EEb9e3f84b5543F74E24e7E1b"],
        interval: StreamingInterval.ONE_MINUTE,
        timeframe: StreamingTimeframe.ONE_HOUR,
      },
      {
        next: (data) => {
          console.log("Received OHLCV token data:", data);
        },
        error: (error) => {
          console.error("Streaming error:", error);
        },
        complete: () => {
          console.log("Stream completed");
        },
      }
    );
    

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/quickstart#response-format)

Response Format
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here is an example of the response you should receive from the above code samples:

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "data": {
        "ohlcvCandlesForToken": [\
          {\
            "chain_name": "BASE_MAINNET",\
            "interval": "ONE_MINUTE",\
            "timeframe": "ONE_HOUR",\
            "timestamp": "2025-06-27T22:24:00Z",\
            "open": 0.000604418526534047,\
            "high": 0.000604638206820701,\
            "low": 0.000604013151624892,\
            "close": 0.000604638206820701,\
            "volume": 1.4980526133065126,\
            "volume_usd": 6004669.256018968,\
            "quote_rate": 0.000604638206820701,\
            "quote_rate_usd": 4007551.6142841205,\
            "base_token": {\
              "contract_name": "Virtual Protocol",\
              "contract_address": "0x0b3e328455c4059eeb9e3f84b5543f74e24e7e1b",\
              "contract_decimals": 18,\
              "contract_ticker_symbol": "VIRTUAL"\
            }\
          }\
        ]
      }
    }

# Authentication - GoldRush API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/authentication#content-area)

[GoldRush API Documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=97917fde1507b0c14e79b83959fe1160)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=5bd4f921dcc81186bf369e7b33ec5734)](https://goldrush.dev/docs)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

GoldRush Streaming API

Authentication

[Overview](https://goldrush.dev/docs/overview)
[Foundational API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/overview)
[Streaming API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/overview)
[Chains](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/overview)

On this page

*   [Why is Authentication Required?](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/authentication#why-is-authentication-required)
    
*   [1\. Obtaining a GoldRush API Key](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/authentication#1-obtaining-a-goldrush-api-key)
    
*   [2\. Supplying the API Key from the Client](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/authentication#2-supplying-the-api-key-from-the-client)
    
*   [Use the GoldRush Client SDK (recommended)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/authentication#use-the-goldrush-client-sdk-recommended)
    
*   [Use a GraphQL WebSocket Client](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/authentication#use-a-graphql-websocket-client)
    
*   [Use websocat for Manual WebSocket Testing](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/authentication#use-websocat-for-manual-websocket-testing)
    
*   [3\. Server-Side Authentication Process](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/authentication#3-server-side-authentication-process)
    
*   [4\. Error Handling](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/authentication#4-error-handling)
    
*   [5\. Frequently Asked Questions (FAQ)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/authentication#5-frequently-asked-questions-faq)
    

This document provides a comprehensive overview of the authentication process for GraphQL subscriptions with the Streaming API. It covers the rationale for authentication, how to obtain and use an API key, client-side implementation examples, server-side validation, error handling, and frequently asked questions.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/authentication#why-is-authentication-required)

Why is Authentication Required?
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Authentication is essential to ensure that only authorized users can access premium or rate-limited real-time data streams. **All clients must present a valid GoldRush API key to interact with the GraphQL subscription endpoints.**

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/authentication#1-obtaining-a-goldrush-api-key)

1\. Obtaining a GoldRush API Key
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To begin, register for an API key at [GoldRush API Dashboard](https://goldrush.dev/platform/auth/register/)
. This key will be required for all authenticated requests to the Streaming API.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/authentication#2-supplying-the-api-key-from-the-client)

2\. Supplying the API Key from the Client
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/authentication#use-the-goldrush-client-sdk-recommended)

Use the GoldRush Client SDK (recommended)

The recommended approach is to use the official [GoldRush TypeScript Client SDK](https://www.npmjs.com/package/@covalenthq/client-sdk)
 which handles authentication automatically and provides a simplified interface for managing stream subscriptions.

Copy

Ask AI

    npm install @covalenthq/client-sdk
    

Copy

Ask AI

    import {
      GoldRushClient,
      StreamingChain,
      StreamingInterval,
      StreamingTimeframe
    } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    const client = new GoldRushClient(
      "<YOUR_API_KEY>", // Your GoldRush API key
      {},
      {
        onConnecting: () => console.log("Connecting to streaming service..."),
        onOpened: () => console.log("Connected to streaming service!"),
        onClosed: () => console.log("Disconnected from streaming service"),
        onError: (error) => console.error("Streaming error:", error),
      }
    );
    
    // Subscribe to OHLCV tokens stream
    client.StreamingService.subscribeToOHLCVTokens(
      {
        chain_name: StreamingChain.BASE_MAINNET,
        token_addresses: ["0x0b3e328455c4059EEb9e3f84b5543F74E24e7E1b"],
        interval: StreamingInterval.ONE_MINUTE,
        timeframe: StreamingTimeframe.ONE_HOUR,
      },
      {
        next: (data) => {
          console.log("Received OHLCV token data:", data);
        },
        error: (error) => {
          console.error("Streaming error:", error);
        },
        complete: () => {
          console.log("Stream completed");
        },
      }
    );
    

The SDK automatically handles:

*   WebSocket connection management
*   API key authentication
*   Connection retry logic
*   Error handling
*   Type safety for parameters

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/authentication#use-a-graphql-websocket-client)

Use a GraphQL WebSocket Client

For direct WebSocket connections, you can use a package like [graphql-ws](https://github.com/enisdenjo/graphql-ws)
 library. Below is an example implementation in Node.js:

Copy

Ask AI

    import { createClient } from "graphql-ws";
    
    const client = createClient({
      url: "wss://gr-staging-v2.streaming.covalenthq.com/graphql",
      connectionParams: {
        GOLDRUSH_API_KEY: "YOUR_API_KEY_HERE", // Replace with your GoldRush API key
      },
    });
    
    (async () => {
      await client.subscribe(
        {
          query: `subscription { newPairs { ...fields } }`,
        },
        {
          next: (data) => console.log("Received data:", data),
          error: (err) => console.error("Subscription error:", err),
          complete: () => console.log("Subscription complete"),
        }
      );
    })();
    

> **Note:** The API key must be provided as `GOLDRUSH_API_KEY` within the `connectionParams` object.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/authentication#use-websocat-for-manual-websocket-testing)

Use `websocat` for Manual WebSocket Testing

For manual testing or debugging, [websocat](https://github.com/vi/websocat)
 can be used to interact with the WebSocket endpoint directly from the command line.

1

Step 1: Initiate the WebSocket Connection

Copy

Ask AI

    websocat -H="Sec-WebSocket-Protocol: graphql-transport-ws" wss://gr-staging-v2.streaming.covalenthq.com/graphql
    

2

Step 2: Send the Connection Initialization Payload

Send the following JSON as your first message, replacing `<YOUR_API_KEY>` with your actual API key:

Copy

Ask AI

    {
        "type": "connection_init",
        "payload": { "GOLDRUSH_API_KEY": "<YOUR_API_KEY>" }
    }
    

Wait for a `connection_ack` response from the server before proceeding.

3

Step 3: Submit a Subscription Query

You may now send a subscription query, for example:

Copy

Ask AI

    {
        "id": "74bb224c-22c6-4a0f-ad85-d43a8c4e49ce",
        "type": "subscribe",
        "payload": {
            "query": "subscription {newPairs(chain_name: BASE_MAINNET) { chain_name protocol protocol_version event_name tx_hash block_signed_at pair_address pair_metadata { contract_name contract_address contract_decimals contract_ticker_symbol } base_token_metadata { contract_name contract_address contract_decimals contract_ticker_symbol } quote_token_metadata { contract_name contract_address contract_decimals contract_ticker_symbol } deployer_address quote_rate quote_rate_usd liquidity market_cap supply prices { last_5m last_1hr last_6hr last_24hr } swaps { last_5m last_1hr last_6hr last_24hr }}}"
        }
    }
    

If authentication is successful, you will begin receiving real-time data for your subscription.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/authentication#3-server-side-authentication-process)

3\. Server-Side Authentication Process
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The server **does not** validate the API key at the time of WebSocket connection establishment.
*   Instead, authentication is enforced at the start of each GraphQL subscription resolver.
*   If the API key is missing or invalid, the subscription will immediately terminate with an error message.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/authentication#4-error-handling)

4\. Error Handling
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If authentication fails, the client will receive a GraphQL error with one of the following codes:

*   `MISSING_TOKEN`: No API key was provided in the `connection_init` payload.
*   `INVALID_TOKEN`: The provided API key is malformed or invalid.
*   `AUTH_SYSTEM_ERROR`: An internal server error occurred during authentication.

**Example Error Response:**

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "errors": [\
        {\
          "message": "Authentication required. Please provide a valid API key in the connection_init payload under 'GOLDRUSH_API_KEY' or 'Authorization' key.",\
          "extensions": {\
            "code": "MISSING_TOKEN"\
          }\
        }\
      ]
    }
    

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/authentication#5-frequently-asked-questions-faq)

5\. Frequently Asked Questions (FAQ)
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **What is the client experience if the key is invalid?**
    *   The client will always receive a `connection_ack` response, even if the API key is invalid. Authentication errors are only reported when a subscription is initiated.
*   **Where is the API key expected?**
    *   The API key is expected in the `payload` of the `connection_init` message with the key `GOLDRUSH_API_KEY`.
*   **What API key formats are supported?**
    *   `cqt_wF[26 base58 chars]` or `cqt_rQ[26 base58 chars]`
*   **Why should I use the Client SDK?**
    *   The Client SDK provides automatic authentication, connection management, retry logic, type safety, and a simplified API for all streaming operations.

[Quickstart](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/quickstart)
[SDK Guide](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/sdk)

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-balances-for-address#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-balances-for-address#parameter-chain-name)

chainName

string

required

The chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-balances-for-address#parameter-wallet-address)

walletAddress

string

required

The requested address. Passing in an `ENS`, `RNS`, `Lens Handle`, or an `Unstoppable Domain` resolves automatically.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-balances-for-address#parameter-quote-currency)

quote-currency

string

The currency to convert. Supports `USD`, `CAD`, `EUR`, `SGD`, `INR`, `JPY`, `VND`, `CNY`, `KRW`, `RUB`, `TRY`, `NGN`, `ARS`, `AUD`, `CHF`, and `GBP`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-balances-for-address#parameter-no-spam)

no-spam

boolean

If `true`, the suspected spam tokens are removed. Supported on all Foundational Chains.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-balances-for-address#response-address)

address

string

The requested address.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-balances-for-address#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-balances-for-address#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-balances-for-address#response-chain-tip-height)

chain\_tip\_height

integer

The latest block height of the blockchain at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-balances-for-address#response-chain-tip-signed-at)

chain\_tip\_signed\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp of the latest signed block at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-balances-for-address#response-quote-currency)

quote\_currency

string

The requested quote currency eg: `USD`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-balances-for-address#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-balances-for-address#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

[Get historical token balances for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address)

# Get Bitcoin balance for non-HD address - GoldRush API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balance-for-address#content-area)

GoldRush SDK

TypeScript

Copy

Ask AI

    import { GoldRushClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    const ApiServices = async () => {
        const client = new GoldRushClient("YOUR_API_KEY");
        const resp = await client.BalanceService.getBitcoinBalanceForWalletAddress({chainName: "chainName", walletAddress: "walletAddress"});
        console.log(resp.data);
    };
    
    ApiServices();

Credit Cost
-----------

1 per call

Processing
----------

Realtime

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balance-for-address#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balance-for-address#parameter-wallet-address)

walletAddress

string

required

The requested bitcoin non-HD address.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balance-for-address#parameter-quote-currency)

quote-currency

string

The currency to convert. Supports `USD`, `CAD`, `EUR`, `SGD`, `INR`, `JPY`, `VND`, `CNY`, `KRW`, `RUB`, `TRY`, `NGN`, `ARS`, `AUD`, `CHF`, and `GBP`.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balance-for-address#response-address)

address

string

The requested address.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balance-for-address#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balance-for-address#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balance-for-address#response-chain-tip-height)

chain\_tip\_height

integer

The latest block height of the blockchain at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balance-for-address#response-chain-tip-signed-at)

chain\_tip\_signed\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp of the latest signed block at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balance-for-address#response-quote-currency)

quote\_currency

string

The requested quote currency eg: `USD`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balance-for-address#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balance-for-address#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

[Get Bitcoin balances for HD address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balances-for-hd-address)
[Get historical Bitcoin balance for non-HD address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-bitcoin-balance-for-address)

        const resp = await client.TransactionService.getTransactionSummary({chainName: "chainName", walletAddress: "walletAddress"});

    };
    
    ApiServices();

Credit Cost
-----------

1 per call

Processing
----------

Batch

*   Base cost is `1` credit.
*   Using `with-gas` is an additional `1` credit.
*   Using `with-transfer-count` is an additional `3` credits.

Related guides

[Building Web3 Wallets (Part 7) - Multi-Chain Wallet Activity Summary](https://goldrush.dev/guides/building-web3-wallets-part-7-multi-chain-wallet-activity-summary)
[How Token Gating and Membership dApps Use the GoldRush API](https://goldrush.dev/guides/how-token-gating-dapps-use-the-covalent-api)
[Comparing GoldRush’s Transactions API to RPC Providers](https://goldrush.dev/guides/comparing-covalent-s-transactions-api-to-rpc-providers)
[How to Get Transaction History for an Address on Ethereum](https://goldrush.dev/guides/how-to-get-transaction-history-for-an-address-on-ethereum)

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-transaction-summary-for-address#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-transaction-summary-for-address#parameter-chain-name)

chainName

string

required

The chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-transaction-summary-for-address#parameter-wallet-address)

walletAddress

string

required

The requested address. Passing in an `ENS`, `RNS`, `Lens Handle`, or an `Unstoppable Domain` resolves automatically.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-transaction-summary-for-address#parameter-quote-currency)

quote-currency

string

The currency to convert. Supports `USD`, `CAD`, `EUR`, `SGD`, `INR`, `JPY`, `VND`, `CNY`, `KRW`, `RUB`, `TRY`, `NGN`, `ARS`, `AUD`, `CHF`, and `GBP`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-transaction-summary-for-address#parameter-with-gas)

with-gas

boolean

Include gas summary details. Response times may be impacted for wallets with large number of transactions.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-transaction-summary-for-address#parameter-with-transfer-count)

with-transfer-count

boolean

Represents the total count of ERC-20 token movement events, including `Transfer`, `Deposit` and `Withdraw`. Response times may be impacted for wallets with large number of transactions.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-transaction-summary-for-address#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-transaction-summary-for-address#response-address)

address

string

The requested address.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-transaction-summary-for-address#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-transaction-summary-for-address#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-transaction-summary-for-address#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

[Get a transaction](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-a-transaction)
[Get earliest transactions for address (v3)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-earliest-transactions-for-address-v3)

# New DEX Pairs Stream - GoldRush API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/new-dex-pairs-stream#content-area)

[GoldRush API Documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=97917fde1507b0c14e79b83959fe1160)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=5bd4f921dcc81186bf369e7b33ec5734)](https://goldrush.dev/docs)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Available Streams

New DEX Pairs Stream

[Overview](https://goldrush.dev/docs/overview)
[Foundational API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/overview)
[Streaming API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/overview)
[Chains](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/overview)

On this page

*   [Parameters](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/new-dex-pairs-stream#parameters)
    
*   [Subscription](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/new-dex-pairs-stream#subscription)
    
*   [Basic Subscription Query](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/new-dex-pairs-stream#basic-subscription-query)
    
*   [Complete Subscription Query](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/new-dex-pairs-stream#complete-subscription-query)
    
*   [Response Format](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/new-dex-pairs-stream#response-format)
    
*   [Field Descriptions](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/new-dex-pairs-stream#field-descriptions)
    

The New DEX Pairs stream provides real-time updates when **new liquidity pairs** are created on decentralized exchanges (DEXes). This documentation follows our standard streaming API structure.

Credit Cost
-----------

TBD

Supported Chains
----------------

*   `BASE_MAINNET`
*   `BSC_MAINNET`
*   `ETH_MAINNET`
*   `SONIC_MAINNET`
*   `SOLANA_MAINNET`
*   `MONAD_MAINNET`

**This stream is currently in Beta.** It is stable for testing and evaluation but may undergo changes in schema or behavior as we continue to improve it. **No API credits are currently charged.**We welcome your feedback so please [reach out](https://goldrush.dev/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#ee9d9b9e9e819c9aae8d81988f828b809a869fc08d8183)
 to us directly to report issues or request features.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/new-dex-pairs-stream#parameters)

Parameters
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `chain_name` | `enum` | Yes | Chain name to filter events (e.g., `BASE_MAINNET`, `ETH_MAINNET`, `BSC_MAINNET`, `SOLANA_MAINNET`) |
| `protocols` | `array<enum>` | Yes | List of protocol name enums to filter events (e.g.,`[UNISWAP_V2, RAYDIUM_AMM]`); see [supported DEXes](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/overview#supported-chains-%26-dexes)<br> for the full list. |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/new-dex-pairs-stream#subscription)

Subscription
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can subscribe to the `newPairs` endpoint to receive events.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/new-dex-pairs-stream#basic-subscription-query)

Basic Subscription Query

Copy

Ask AI

    subscription {
      newPairs(chain_name: BASE_MAINNET, protocols: [UNISWAP_V2, UNISWAP_V3]) {
        chain_name
        protocol
        protocol_version
        tx_hash
        block_signed_at
      }
    }
    

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/new-dex-pairs-stream#complete-subscription-query)

Complete Subscription Query

Copy

Ask AI

    subscription {
      newPairs(chain_name: BASE_MAINNET, protocols: [UNISWAP_V2, UNISWAP_V3]) {
        chain_name
        protocol
        protocol_version
        pair_address
        deployer_address
        tx_hash
        block_signed_at
        liquidity
        supply
        market_cap
        event_name
        quote_rate
        quote_rate_usd
        base_token_metadata {
          contract_address
          contract_decimals
          contract_name
          contract_ticker_symbol
        }
        pair_metadata {
          contract_address
          contract_decimals
          contract_name
          contract_ticker_symbol
        }
        quote_token_metadata {
          contract_address
          contract_decimals
          contract_name
          contract_ticker_symbol
        }
      }
    }
    

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/new-dex-pairs-stream#response-format)

Response Format
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here’s an example of the response data structure:

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "data": {
        "newPairs": [\
          {\
            "chain_name": "base",\
            "protocol": "uniswap",\
            "protocol_version": "3",\
            "pair_address": "0xa7dfb58a6e0d675c19f76dfd3b8b80a3a4814728",\
            "deployer_address": "0x33128a8fc17869897dce68ed026d694621f6fdfd",\
            "tx_hash": "0x5374c0182580ff2b3e868f58bdce697f3e4256baebc6f6e8db008fadb32d6253",\
            "block_signed_at": "2025-05-28T22:01:41Z",\
            "liquidity": 177.50267302070574,\
            "supply": 1000000000,\
            "market_cap": 6153.261270529,\
            "event_name": "PoolCreated",\
            "quote_rate": 0.000006153261270529,\
            "quote_rate_usd": 0.000006153261270529,\
            "base_token_metadata": {\
              "contract_address": "0x8ac05571b525dd555320df58a40a0c0ab6d807c7",\
              "contract_decimals": 18,\
              "contract_name": "GOAT",\
              "contract_ticker_symbol": "GOAT"\
            },\
            "quote_token_metadata": {\
              "contract_address": "0x1111111111166b7fe7bd91427724b487980afc69",\
              "contract_decimals": 18,\
              "contract_name": "Zora",\
              "contract_ticker_symbol": "ZORA"\
            },\
            "pair_metadata": {\
              "contract_address": "0xa7dfb58a6e0d675c19f76dfd3b8b80a3a4814728",\
              "contract_decimals": 18,\
              "contract_name": "GOAT-ZORA Pool",\
              "contract_ticker_symbol": "GOAT-ZORA"\
            },\
          }\
        ]
      }
    }
    

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/new-dex-pairs-stream#field-descriptions)

Field Descriptions

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `chain_name` | `string` | The blockchain network where the pair was created |
| `protocol` | `string` | DEX protocol name (e.g., “uniswap”, “pancakeswap”) |
| `protocol_version` | `string` | Version of the DEX protocol |
| `pair_address` | `string` | Address of the new pair contract |
| `deployer_address` | `string` | Address that deployed the pair contract |
| `tx_hash` | `string` | Transaction hash of the pair creation |
| `block_signed_at` | `string` | ISO timestamp of when the block was signed |
| `liquidity` | `float` | Initial liquidity amount (in USD) |
| `supply` | `integer` | Total supply of the pair token |
| `market_cap` | `float` | Market capitalization in USD |
| `event_name` | `string` | Name of the contract event (e.g., “PoolCreated”) |
| `quote_rate` | `float` | Exchange rate between base and quote tokens |
| `quote_rate_usd` | `float` | USD value of the quote rate |
| `base_token_metadata` | `object` | Metadata for the base token including contract address, decimals, name, and symbol |
| `quote_token_metadata` | `object` | Metadata for the quote token including contract address, decimals, name, and symbol |
| `pair_metadata` | `object` | Metadata for the pair including contract address, decimals, name, and symbol |

[OHLCV Pairs Stream](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-pairs-stream)
[Update Pairs Stream](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/update-pairs-stream)

⌘I

# Get NFTs for address - GoldRush API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/get-nfts-for-address#content-area)

GoldRush SDK

TypeScript

Copy

Ask AI

    import { GoldRushClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    const ApiServices = async () => {
        const client = new GoldRushClient("YOUR_API_KEY");
        const resp = await client.NftService.getNftsForAddress({chainName: "chainName", walletAddress: "walletAddress"});
        console.log(resp.data);
    };
    
    ApiServices();

    };
    
    ApiServices();

-----------

1 per call

Processing
----------

Realtime

Related guides

[Displaying NFT Holdings with GoldRush’s NFT Endpoints](https://goldrush.dev/guides/from-wallet-to-web-displaying-nft-holdings-with-covalent-s-nft-endpoints)

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/get-nfts-for-address#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/get-nfts-for-address#parameter-chain-name)

chainName

string

required

The chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/get-nfts-for-address#parameter-wallet-address)

walletAddress

string

required

The requested address. Passing in an `ENS`, `RNS`, `Lens Handle`, or an `Unstoppable Domain` resolves automatically.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/get-nfts-for-address#parameter-no-spam)

no-spam

boolean

If `true`, the suspected spam tokens are removed. Supported on all Foundational Chains.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/get-nfts-for-address#parameter-no-nft-asset-metadata)

no-nft-asset-metadata

boolean

If `true`, the response shape is limited to a list of collections and token ids, omitting metadata and asset information. Helpful for faster response times and wallets holding a large number of NFTs.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/get-nfts-for-address#response-address)

address

string

The requested address.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/get-nfts-for-address#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/get-nfts-for-address#response-chain-tip-height)

chain\_tip\_height

integer

The latest block height of the blockchain at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/get-nfts-for-address#response-chain-tip-signed-at)

chain\_tip\_signed\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp of the latest signed block at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/get-nfts-for-address#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

[Get all transactions in a block (v3)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block)
[Check ownership in NFT collection](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/check-ownership-in-nft-collection)

# OHLCV Tokens Stream - GoldRush API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-tokens-stream#content-area)

[GoldRush API Documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=97917fde1507b0c14e79b83959fe1160)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=5bd4f921dcc81186bf369e7b33ec5734)](https://goldrush.dev/docs)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Available Streams

OHLCV Tokens Stream

[Overview](https://goldrush.dev/docs/overview)
[Foundational API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/overview)
[Streaming API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/overview)
[Chains](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/overview)

On this page

*   [Parameters](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-tokens-stream#parameters)
    
*   [Subscription](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-tokens-stream#subscription)
    
*   [Basic Subscription Query](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-tokens-stream#basic-subscription-query)
    
*   [Complete Subscription Query](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-tokens-stream#complete-subscription-query)
    
*   [Response Format](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-tokens-stream#response-format)
    
*   [Field Descriptions](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-tokens-stream#field-descriptions)
    

The OHLCV Tokens stream provides real-time updates on the Open, High, Low, Close prices and Volume of **one or many tokens** at configurable intervals. This documentation follows our standard streaming API structure.

Credit Cost
-----------

TBD

Supported Chains
----------------

*   `BASE_MAINNET`
*   `BSC_MAINNET`
*   `ETH_MAINNET`
*   `SONIC_MAINNET`
*   `SOLANA_MAINNET`
*   `HYPERCORE_MAINNET`
*   `MONAD_MAINNET`

**This stream is currently in Beta.** It is stable for testing and evaluation but may undergo changes in schema or behavior as we continue to improve it. **No API credits are currently charged.**We welcome your feedback so please [reach out](https://goldrush.dev/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#cdbeb8bdbda2bfb98daea2bbaca1a8a3b9a5bce3aea2a0)
 to us directly to report issues or request features.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-tokens-stream#parameters)

Parameters
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `chain_name` | `enum` | Yes | Chain name to filter events (e.g. `BASE_MAINNET`, `ETH_MAINNET`, `BSC_MAINNET`, `SOLANA_MAINNET`) |
| `token_addresses` | `array<string>` | Yes | Array of token addresses on [supported DEXes](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/overview#supported-chains-%26-dexes)<br> and chains to track |
| `interval` | `enum` | Yes | Frequency of OHLCV data updates, ranging from sub-second to one day |
| `timeframe` | `enum` | Yes | Historical lookback period for OHLCV data, ranging from one minute to one month |
| `limit` | `int` | No  | Maximum number of items returned per stream message to control payload size |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-tokens-stream#subscription)

Subscription
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can subscribe to the `ohlcvCandlesForToken` endpoint to receive the pricing events.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-tokens-stream#basic-subscription-query)

Basic Subscription Query

Copy

Ask AI

    subscription {
      ohlcvCandlesForToken(
        chain_name: BASE_MAINNET
        token_addresses: ["0x4B6104755AfB5Da4581B81C552DA3A25608c73B8"]
        interval: ONE_MINUTE
        timeframe: ONE_HOUR
      ) {
        chain_name
        interval
        timeframe
        timestamp
        open
        high
        low
        close
        volume
        volume_usd
        quote_rate
        quote_rate_usd
        base_token {
          contract_name
          contract_address
          contract_decimals
          contract_ticker_symbol
        }
      }
    }
    

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-tokens-stream#complete-subscription-query)

Complete Subscription Query

Copy

Ask AI

    subscription {
      ohlcvCandlesForToken(
        chain_name: BASE_MAINNET
        token_addresses: [\
          "0x4B6104755AfB5Da4581B81C552DA3A25608c73B8"\
        ]
        interval: ONE_MINUTE
        timeframe: ONE_HOUR
        limit: 1000
      ) {
        chain_name
        pair_address
        interval
        timeframe
        timestamp
        open
        high
        low
        close
        volume
        volume_usd
        quote_rate
        quote_rate_usd
        base_token {
          contract_name
          contract_address
          contract_decimals
          contract_ticker_symbol
        }
        quote_token {
          contract_name
          contract_address
          contract_decimals
          contract_ticker_symbol
        }
      }
    }
    

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-tokens-stream#response-format)

Response Format
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here’s an example of the response data structure:

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "data": {
        "ohlcvCandlesForToken": [\
          {\
            "chain_name": "BASE_MAINNET",\
            "interval": "ONE_MINUTE",\
            "timeframe": "ONE_HOUR",\
            "timestamp": "2025-06-27T22:24:00Z",\
            "open": 0.000604418526534047,\
            "high": 0.000604638206820701,\
            "low": 0.000604013151624892,\
            "close": 0.000604638206820701,\
            "volume": 1.4980526133065126,\
            "volume_usd": 6004669.256018968,\
            "quote_rate": 0.000604638206820701,\
            "quote_rate_usd": 4007551.6142841205,\
            "base_token": {\
              "contract_name": "Virtual Protocol",\
              "contract_address": "0x0b3e328455c4059eeb9e3f84b5543f74e24e7e1b",\
              "contract_decimals": 18,\
              "contract_ticker_symbol": "VIRTUAL"\
            }\
          }\
        ]
      }
    }
    

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-tokens-stream#field-descriptions)

Field Descriptions

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `chain_name` | `string` | The blockchain network where the token exists |
| `pair_address` | `string` | The address of the primary DEX pool with the most liquidity for the token |
| `interval` | `enum` | The candle interval |
| `timeframe` | `enum` | The requested timeframe |
| `timestamp` | `string` | ISO timestamp for the candle |
| `open` | `float` | Opening price for the interval |
| `high` | `float` | Highest price during the interval |
| `low` | `float` | Lowest price during the interval |
| `close` | `float` | Closing price for the interval |
| `volume` | `float` | Trading volume during the interval |
| `volume_usd` | `float` | Trading volume in USD |
| `quote_rate` | `float` | Exchange rate between base and quote tokens |
| `quote_rate_usd` | `float` | USD value of the quote rate |
| `base_token` | `object` | Information about the queried token |
| `quote_token` | `object` | Information about the paired token of the primary DEX pool |

[SDK Guide](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/sdk)
[OHLCV Pairs Stream](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-pairs-stream)

# Get top trading wallets for token - GoldRush API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token#content-area)

[GoldRush API Documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=97917fde1507b0c14e79b83959fe1160)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=5bd4f921dcc81186bf369e7b33ec5734)](https://goldrush.dev/docs)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Available Queries

Get top trading wallets for token

[Overview](https://goldrush.dev/docs/overview)
[Foundational API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/overview)
[Streaming API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/overview)
[Chains](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/overview)

On this page

*   [Parameters](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token#parameters)
    
*   [Query](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token#query)
    
*   [Basic Query](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token#basic-query)
    
*   [Complete Query](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token#complete-query)
    
*   [Response Format](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token#response-format)
    
*   [Field Descriptions](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token#field-descriptions)
    
*   [GraphQL Playground](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token#graphql-playground)
    

This GraphQL query provides a list of wallets with the highest trading volume for a specific token over the last 30 days, along with detailed information about their holdings, transaction activity, realized and unrealized profit/loss metrics. This documentation follows our standard streaming API structure.

Credit Cost
-----------

TBD

Supported Chains
----------------

*   Base Mainnet
*   BSC Mainnet
*   Ethereum Mainnet
*   Gnosis Mainnet
*   Polygon Mainnet
*   Optimism Mainnet

**This query is currently in Beta.** It is stable for testing and evaluation but may undergo changes in schema or behavior as we continue to improve it. **No API credits are currently charged.**We welcome your feedback so please [reach out](https://goldrush.dev/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#21525451514e535561424e57404d444f5549500f424e4c)
 to us directly to report issues or request features.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token#parameters)

Parameters
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `chain_name` | `enum` | Yes | Chain name to filter events (e.g., `BASE_MAINNET`, `ETH_MAINNET`, `BSC_MAINNET`) |
| `token_address` | `string` | Yes | The deployed token contract address to query |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token#query)

Query
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can query the `upnlForToken` endpoint to retrieve top wallet trading data.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token#basic-query)

Basic Query

Copy

Ask AI

    query {
     upnlForToken(
        chain_name: ETH_MAINNET
        token_address: "0x7ABc8A5768E6bE61A6c693a6e4EAcb5B60602C4D"
      ) {
        token
        address
        volume
        balance
        pnl_realized_usd
        pnl_unrealized_usd
      }
    }
    
    

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token#complete-query)

Complete Query

Copy

Ask AI

    query {
     upnlForToken(
        chain_name: ETH_MAINNET
        token_address: "0x7ABc8A5768E6bE61A6c693a6e4EAcb5B60602C4D"
      ) {
        token
        address
        volume
        transactions_count
        pnl_realized_usd
        balance
        balance_pretty
        pnl_unrealized_usd
        contract_metadata {
          contract_address
          contract_name
          contract_ticker_symbol
          contract_decimals
        }
      }
    }
    
    

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token#response-format)

Response Format
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here’s an example of the response data structure:

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "data": {
        "upnlForToken": [\
          {\
            "token": "0x7abc8a5768e6be61a6c693a6e4eacb5b60602c4d",\
            "address": "0x91d40e4818f4d4c57b4578d9eca6afc92ac8debe",\
            "volume": 56708716,\
            "transactions_count": 554,\
            "pnl_realized_usd": -43239.81,\
            "balance": 3.2944375440228563e+25,\
            "balance_pretty": "32944375.4402",\
            "pnl_unrealized_usd": 535182,\
            "contract_metadata": {\
              "contract_address": "0x7ABc8A5768E6bE61A6c693a6e4EAcb5B60602C4D",\
              "contract_name": "Covalent X Token",\
              "contract_ticker_symbol": "CXT",\
              "contract_decimals": 18\
            }\
          },\
          {\
            "token": "0x7abc8a5768e6be61a6c693a6e4eacb5b60602c4d",\
            "address": "0xfe97b0c517a84f98fc6ede3cd26b43012d31992a",\
            "volume": 39102028,\
            "transactions_count": 241,\
            "pnl_realized_usd": 8799.58,\
            "balance": 3.2313896033867796e+26,\
            "balance_pretty": "323138960.3387",\
            "pnl_unrealized_usd": 6417132,\
            "contract_metadata": {\
              "contract_address": "0x7ABc8A5768E6bE61A6c693a6e4EAcb5B60602C4D",\
              "contract_name": "Covalent X Token",\
              "contract_ticker_symbol": "CXT",\
              "contract_decimals": 18\
            }\
          }\
        ]
      }
    }
    

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token#field-descriptions)

Field Descriptions

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `token` | `string` | Token contract address, represented in lowercase with a 0x prefix |
| `address` | `string` | Wallet address of the token trader, also in lowercase with a 0x prefix |
| `volume` | `BigInteger` | Total volume of tokens transferred by this wallet in the past 30 days |
| `transactions_count` | `integer` | Number of transactions involving this wallet and token in the past 30 days |
| `pnl_realized_usd` | `float` | Realized profit or loss in USD from completed trades |
| `balance` | `BigInteger` | Current token balance in raw format (full decimal precision) |
| `balance_pretty` | `string` | Human-readable token balance formatted to 4 decimal places |
| `pnl_unrealized_usd` | `float` | Unrealized profit or loss in USD based on the current token price |
| `contract_metadata` | `object` | Contains metadata details for the token contract |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token#graphql-playground)

GraphQL Playground
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Wallet Activity Stream](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/wallet-activity-stream)
[Get PnL for wallet](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-wallet)

⌘I

# OHLCV Pairs Stream - GoldRush API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-pairs-stream#content-area)

[GoldRush API Documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=97917fde1507b0c14e79b83959fe1160)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=5bd4f921dcc81186bf369e7b33ec5734)](https://goldrush.dev/docs)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Available Streams

OHLCV Pairs Stream

[Overview](https://goldrush.dev/docs/overview)
[Foundational API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/overview)
[Streaming API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/overview)
[Chains](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/overview)

On this page

*   [Parameters](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-pairs-stream#parameters)
    
*   [Subscription](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-pairs-stream#subscription)
    
*   [Basic Subscription Query](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-pairs-stream#basic-subscription-query)
    
*   [Complete Subscription Query](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-pairs-stream#complete-subscription-query)
    
*   [Response Format](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-pairs-stream#response-format)
    
*   [Field Descriptions](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-pairs-stream#field-descriptions)
    

The OHLCV Pairs stream provides real-time updates on the Open, High, Low, Close prices and Volume of **one or many token pairs** at configurable intervals. This documentation follows our standard streaming API structure.

Credit Cost
-----------

TBD

Supported Chains
----------------

*   `BASE_MAINNET`
*   `BSC_MAINNET`
*   `ETH_MAINNET`
*   `SOLANA_MAINNET`
*   `SONIC_MAINNET`
*   `MONAD_MAINNET`

**This stream is currently in Beta.** It is stable for testing and evaluation but may undergo changes in schema or behavior as we continue to improve it. **No API credits are currently charged.**We welcome your feedback so please [reach out](https://goldrush.dev/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#bac9cfcacad5c8cefad9d5ccdbd6dfd4ced2cb94d9d5d7)
 to us directly to report issues or request features.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-pairs-stream#parameters)

Parameters
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `chain_name` | `enum` | Yes | Chain name to filter events (e.g. `BASE_MAINNET`, `ETH_MAINNET`, `BSC_MAINNET`, `SOLANA_MAINNET`) |
| `pair_addresses` | `array<string>` | Yes | Array of pair addresses on [supported DEXes](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/overview#supported-chains-%26-dexes)<br> and chains to track |
| `interval` | `enum` | Yes | Frequency of OHLCV data updates, ranging from sub-second to one day |
| `timeframe` | `enum` | Yes | Historical lookback period for OHLCV data, ranging from one minute to one month |
| `limit` | `int` | No  | Maximum number of items returned per stream message to control payload size |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-pairs-stream#subscription)

Subscription
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can subscribe to the `ohlcvCandlesForPair` endpoint to receive the pricing events.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-pairs-stream#basic-subscription-query)

Basic Subscription Query

Copy

Ask AI

    subscription {
      ohlcvCandlesForPair(
        chain_name: BASE_MAINNET
        pair_addresses: ["0x9c087Eb773291e50CF6c6a90ef0F4500e349B903"]
        interval: ONE_MINUTE
        timeframe: ONE_HOUR
      ) {
        chain_name
        pair_address
        interval
        timeframe
        timestamp
        open
        high
        low
        close
        volume
        volume_usd
        quote_rate
        quote_rate_usd
      }
    }
    

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-pairs-stream#complete-subscription-query)

Complete Subscription Query

Copy

Ask AI

    subscription {
      ohlcvCandlesForPair(
        chain_name: BASE_MAINNET
        pair_addresses: [\
          "0x9c087Eb773291e50CF6c6a90ef0F4500e349B903"\
          "0x4b0Aaf3EBb163dd45F663b38b6d93f6093EBC2d3"\
        ]
        interval: ONE_MINUTE
        timeframe: ONE_HOUR
        limit: 1000
      ) {
        chain_name
        pair_address
        interval
        timeframe
        timestamp
        open
        high
        low
        close
        volume
        volume_usd
        quote_rate
        quote_rate_usd
        base_token {
          contract_name
          contract_address
          contract_decimals
          contract_ticker_symbol
        }
        quote_token {
          contract_name
          contract_address
          contract_decimals
          contract_ticker_symbol
        }
      }
    }
    

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-pairs-stream#response-format)

Response Format
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here’s an example of the response data structure:

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "data": {
        "ohlcvCandlesForPair": [\
          {\
            "chain_name": "BASE_MAINNET",\
            "pair_address": "0x4b0Aaf3EBb163dd45F663b38b6d93f6093EBC2d3",\
            "interval": "ONE_MINUTE",\
            "timeframe": "ONE_HOUR",\
            "timestamp": "2025-05-29T19:53:00Z",\
            "open": 4113151.389790023,\
            "high": 4196665.022060752,\
            "low": 4113151.389790023,\
            "close": 4196665.022060752,\
            "volume": 325.7615900713698,\
            "volume_usd": 0.2079461510855417,\
            "quote_rate": 4196665.022060752,\
            "quote_rate_usd": 0.0006319231563715365,\
            "quote_token": {\
              "contract_name": "Wrapped Ether",\
              "contract_symbol": "WETH",\
              "contract_address": "0x4200000000000000000000000000000000000006",\
              "contract_decimals": 18\
            },\
            "base_token": {\
              "contract_name": "Toshi",\
              "contract_symbol": "TOSHI",\
              "contract_address": "0xac1bd2486aaf3b5c0fc3fd868558b082a531b2b4",\
              "contract_decimals": 18\
            }\
          }\
        ]
      }
    }
    

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-pairs-stream#field-descriptions)

Field Descriptions

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `chain_name` | `string` | The blockchain network where the pair exists |
| `pair_address` | `string` | The address of the DEX pair |
| `interval` | `enum` | The candle interval |
| `timeframe` | `enum` | The requested timeframe |
| `timestamp` | `string` | ISO timestamp for the candle |
| `open` | `float` | Opening price for the interval |
| `high` | `float` | Highest price during the interval |
| `low` | `float` | Lowest price during the interval |
| `close` | `float` | Closing price for the interval |
| `volume` | `float` | Trading volume during the interval |
| `volume_usd` | `float` | Trading volume in USD |
| `quote_rate` | `float` | Exchange rate between base and quote tokens |
| `quote_rate_usd` | `float` | USD value of the quote rate |
| `base_token` | `object` | Information about the base token in the pair |
| `quote_token` | `object` | Information about the quote token in the pair |

[OHLCV Tokens Stream](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-tokens-stream)
[New DEX Pairs Stream](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/new-dex-pairs-stream)

# SDK Guide - GoldRush API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/sdk#content-area)

[GoldRush API Documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=97917fde1507b0c14e79b83959fe1160)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=5bd4f921dcc81186bf369e7b33ec5734)](https://goldrush.dev/docs)

Navigation

GoldRush Streaming API

SDK Guide

[Overview](https://goldrush.dev/docs/overview)
[Foundational API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/overview)
[Streaming API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/overview)
[Chains](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/overview)

On this page

*   [Basic Subscription](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/sdk#basic-subscription)
    
*   [Multiple Subscriptions](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/sdk#multiple-subscriptions)
    
*   [React Integration](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/sdk#react-integration)
    
*   [GraphQL Queries](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/sdk#graphql-queries)
    

With the official [TypeScript Client SDK](https://www.npmjs.com/package/@covalenthq/client-sdk)
, developers can access the Streaming API and leverage the following advanced features described in this guide.

Copy

Ask AI

    npm install @covalenthq/client-sdk
    

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/sdk#basic-subscription)

Basic Subscription
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The following code sample shows how to set up a subscription to the OHLCV Pairs stream:

GoldRush SDK

Copy

Ask AI

    import {
      GoldRushClient,
      StreamingChain,
      StreamingInterval,
      StreamingTimeframe,
      StreamingProtocol,
    } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    const client = new GoldRushClient(
      "<GOLDRUSH_API_KEY>",
      {},
      {
        onConnecting: () => console.log("Connecting to streaming service..."),
        onOpened: () => console.log("Connected to streaming service!"),
        onClosed: () => console.log("Disconnected from streaming service"),
        onError: (error) => console.error("Streaming error:", error),
      }
    );
    
    // Subscribe to OHLCV data for trading pairs
    const unsubscribeOhlcvPairs = client.StreamingService.subscribeToOHLCVPairs(
      {
        chain_name: StreamingChain.BASE_MAINNET,
        pair_addresses: ["0x9c087Eb773291e50CF6c6a90ef0F4500e349B903"],
        interval: StreamingInterval.ONE_MINUTE,
        timeframe: StreamingTimeframe.ONE_HOUR,
      },
      {
        next: (data) => {
          console.log("Received OHLCV pair data:", data);
        },
        error: (error) => {
          console.error("Streaming error:", error);
        },
        complete: () => {
          console.log("Stream completed");
        },
      }
    );
    
    // Unsubscribe when done
    unsubscribeOhlcvPairs();
    
    // Disconnect from streaming service when finished
    await client.StreamingService.disconnect();
    

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/sdk#multiple-subscriptions)

Multiple Subscriptions
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The SDK uses a singleton WebSocket client internally, allowing you to create multiple subscriptions through the same GoldRushClient.

GoldRush SDK

Copy

Ask AI

    import {
      GoldRushClient,
      StreamingChain,
      StreamingInterval,
      StreamingTimeframe,
      StreamingProtocol,
    } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    // Create a single client
    const client = new GoldRushClient(
      "<GOLDRUSH_API_KEY>",
      {},
      {
        onConnecting: () => console.log("Connecting to streaming service..."),
        onOpened: () => console.log("Connected to streaming service!"),
        onClosed: () => console.log("Disconnected from streaming service"),
        onError: (error) => console.error("Streaming error:", error),
      }
    );
    
    // Create multiple subscriptions through the same connection
    const unsubscribePairs = client.StreamingService.subscribeToOHLCVPairs(
      {
        chain_name: StreamingChain.BASE_MAINNET,
        pair_addresses: ["0x9c087Eb773291e50CF6c6a90ef0F4500e349B903"],
        interval: StreamingInterval.ONE_MINUTE,
        timeframe: StreamingTimeframe.ONE_HOUR,
      },
      {
        next: (data) => console.log("OHLCV Pairs:", data),
      }
    );
    
    const unsubscribeTokens = client.StreamingService.subscribeToOHLCVTokens(
      {
        chain_name: StreamingChain.BASE_MAINNET,
        token_addresses: ["0x4B6104755AfB5Da4581B81C552DA3A25608c73B8"],
        interval: StreamingInterval.ONE_MINUTE,
        timeframe: StreamingTimeframe.ONE_HOUR,
      },
      {
        next: (data) => console.log("OHLCV Tokens:", data),
      }
    );
    
    const unsubscribeWallet = client.StreamingService.subscribeToWalletActivity(
      {
        chain_name: StreamingChain.BASE_MAINNET,
        wallet_addresses: ["0xbaed383ede0e5d9d72430661f3285daa77e9439f"],
      },
      {
        next: (data) => console.log("Wallet Activity:", data),
      }
    );
    
    // Unsubscribe from individual streams when needed
    unsubscribePairs();
    unsubscribeTokens();
    unsubscribeWallet();
    
    // Or disconnect from all streams at once
    await client.StreamingService.disconnect();
    

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/sdk#react-integration)

React Integration
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For React applications, use the `useEffect` hook to properly manage subscription lifecycle:

GoldRush SDK

Copy

Ask AI

    useEffect(() => {
      const unsubscribe = client.StreamingService.rawQuery(
        `subscription {
            ohlcvCandlesForPair(
              chain_name: BASE_MAINNET
              pair_addresses: ["0x9c087Eb773291e50CF6c6a90ef0F4500e349B903"],
              interval: StreamingInterval.ONE_MINUTE,
              timeframe: StreamingTimeframe.ONE_HOUR,
            ) {
              open
              high
              low
              close
              volume
              price_usd
              volume_usd
              chain_name
              pair_address
              interval
              timeframe
              timestamp
            }
          }`,
        {},
        {
          next: (data) => console.log("Received streaming data:", data),
          error: (err) => console.error("Subscription error:", err),
          complete: () => console.info("Subscription completed"),
        }
      );
    
      // Cleanup function - unsubscribe when component unmounts
      return () => {
        unsubscribe();
      };
    }, []);
    

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/sdk#graphql-queries)

GraphQL Queries
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can also use raw GraphQL queries for more streamlined and selective data scenarios:

GoldRush SDK

Copy

Ask AI

    const unsubscribeNewPairs = client.StreamingService.rawQuery(
      `subscription {
           newPairs(
             chain_name: BASE_MAINNET,
             protocols: [UNISWAP_V2, UNISWAP_V3]
           ) {
             chain_name
             protocol
             pair_address
             tx_hash
             liquidity
             base_token_metadata {
               contract_name
               contract_ticker_symbol
             }
             quote_token_metadata {
               contract_name
               contract_ticker_symbol
             }
           }
         }`,
      {},
      {
        next: (data) => console.log("Raw new pairs data:", data),
        error: (error) => console.error("Error:", error),
      }
    );
    
    // Raw query for token OHLCV data
    const unsubscribeTokenOHLCV = client.StreamingService.rawQuery(
      `subscription {
          ohlcvCandlesForToken(
            chain_name: BASE_MAINNET
            token_addresses: ["0x4B6104755AfB5Da4581B81C552DA3A25608c73B8"]
            interval: ONE_MINUTE
            timeframe: ONE_HOUR
          ) {
            open
            high
            low
            close
            volume
            volume_usd
            quote_rate
            quote_rate_usd
            timestamp
            base_token {
              contract_name
              contract_ticker_symbol
            }
          }
        }`,
      {},
      {
        next: (data) => console.log("Raw token OHLCV data:", data),
        error: (error) => console.error("Error:", error),
      }
    );
    

[Authentication](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/authentication)

The Update Pairs stream provides real-time updates on the prices, volumes, market cap and liquidity of **one or many token pairs**. This documentation follows our standard streaming API structure.

Credit Cost
-----------

TBD

Supported Chains
----------------

*   `BASE_MAINNET`
*   `BSC_MAINNET`
*   `ETH_MAINNET`
*   `SONIC_MAINNET`
*   `SOLANA_MAINNET`
*   `MONAD_MAINNET`

**This stream is currently in Beta.** It is stable for testing and evaluation but may undergo changes in schema or behavior as we continue to improve it. **No API credits are currently charged.**We welcome your feedback so please [reach out](https://goldrush.dev/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#50232520203f222410333f26313c353e2438217e333f3d)
 to us directly to report issues or request features.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/update-pairs-stream#parameters)

Parameters
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `chain_name` | `enum` | Yes | Chain name to filter events (e.g. `BASE_MAINNET`, `ETH_MAINNET`, `BSC_MAINNET`, `SOLANA_MAINNET`) |
| `pair_addresses` | `array<string>` | Yes | Array of pair addresses on [supported DEXes](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/overview#supported-chains-%26-dexes)<br> and chains to track |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/update-pairs-stream#subscription)

Subscription
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can subscribe to the `updatePairs` endpoint to receive the events.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/update-pairs-stream#basic-subscription-query)

Basic Subscription Query

Copy

Ask AI

    subscription {
      updatePairs(
        chain_name: BASE_MAINNET
        pair_addresses: ["0x9c087Eb773291e50CF6c6a90ef0F4500e349B903"]
      ) {
        chain_name
        pair_address
        timestamp
        quote_rate
        quote_rate_usd
        volume
        volume_usd
        market_cap
        liquidity
      }
    }
    

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/update-pairs-stream#complete-subscription-query)

Complete Subscription Query

Copy

Ask AI

    subscription {
      updatePairs(
        chain_name: BASE_MAINNET
        pair_addresses: [\
          "0x9c087Eb773291e50CF6c6a90ef0F4500e349B903"\
          "0x4b0Aaf3EBb163dd45F663b38b6d93f6093EBC2d3"\
        ]
      ) {

        pair_address
        timestamp
        quote_rate

          contract_ticker_symbol

          contract_address

          contract_ticker_symbol
        }

          last_5m
          last_1hr
          last_6hr
          last_24hr
        }
        swap_counts {
          last_5m
          last_1hr
          last_6hr
          last_24hr

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/update-pairs-stream#response-format)

Response Format
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here’s an example of the response data structure:

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "data": {
        "updatePairs": [\
          {\
            "chain_name": "BASE_MAINNET",\
            "pair_address": "0x9c087Eb773291e50CF6c6a90ef0F4500e349B903",\
            "quote_rate": 0.0002962,\
            "quote_rate_usd": 1.39,\
            "volume": 0.2079461510855417,\
            "volume_usd": 975.515187,\
            "quote_token": {\
              "contract_name": "Wrapped Ether",\
              "contract_symbol": "WETH",\
              "contract_address": "0x4200000000000000000000000000000000000006",\
              "contract_decimals": 18\
            },\
            "base_token": {\
              "contract_name": "Virtual",\
              "contract_symbol": "VIRTUAL",\
              "contract_address": "0x0b3e328455c4059EEb9e3f84b5543F74E24e7E1b",\
              "contract_decimals": 18\
            },\
            "swap_counts": {\
              "last_5m": 10\
              "last_1hr": 100\
              "last_6hr": 1000\
              "last_24hr": 10000\
            },\
            "price_deltas": {\
              "last_5m": 1.2\
              "last_1hr": 1.9\
              "last_6hr": 2.7\
              "last_24hr": -9.1\
            }\
          }\
        ]
      }
    }
    

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/update-pairs-stream#field-descriptions)

Field Descriptions

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `chain_name` | `string` | The blockchain network where the pair exists |
| `pair_address` | `string` | The address of the DEX pair |
| `quote_rate` | `float` | Quote rate of the token |
| `quote_rate_usd` | `float` | Quote rate of the token in USD |
| `volume` | `float` | Trading volume during the interval |
| `volume_usd` | `float` | Trading volume in USD |
| `base_token` | `object` | Information about the base token in the pair |
| `quote_token` | `object` | Information about the quote token in the pair |
| `swap_counts` | `object` | Swap counts for last 5m, 1hr, 6hr, 24hr |
| `price_deltas` | `object` | Price deltas for last 5m, 1hr, 6hr, 24hr |

[New DEX Pairs Stream](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/new-dex-pairs-stream)
[Wallet Activity Stream](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/wallet-activity-stream)

      ]
    }

Credit Cost
-----------

0.01 per item

Processing
----------

Realtime

Limits:

*   For a block range of 2,000 blocks or less, the response will include all logs within the range.
*   For a block range greater than 2,000 blocks:- The response will include up to 10,000 logs.
*   If the number of logs exceeds 10,000, no logs will be included in the response. Instead, the response will contain a suggested range within the `info` object, including a link and message.

Related guides

[How to Get the Latest Axie Spawns](https://goldrush.dev/guides/how-to-get-the-latest-axie-spawns)

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-logs#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-logs#parameter-chain-name)

chainName

string

required

The chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-logs#parameter-starting-block)

starting-block

integer

The first block to retrieve log events with. Accepts decimals, hexadecimals, or the strings `earliest` and `latest`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-logs#parameter-ending-block)

ending-block

string

The last block to retrieve log events with. Accepts decimals, hexadecimals, or the strings `earliest` and `latest`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-logs#parameter-address)

address

string

The address of the log events sender contract.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-logs#parameter-topics)

topics

string

The topic hash(es) to retrieve logs with.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-logs#parameter-block-hash)

block-hash

string

The block hash to retrieve logs for.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-logs#parameter-skip-decode)

skip-decode

boolean

Omit decoded log events.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-logs#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-logs#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-logs#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-logs#response-chain-tip-height)

chain\_tip\_height

integer

The latest block height of the blockchain at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-logs#response-chain-tip-signed-at)

chain\_tip\_signed\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp of the latest signed block at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-logs#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

[Get gas prices](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-gas-prices)
[Get log events by topic hash(es)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash)

Resources

Decoded Events

On this page

*   [Transfer Event](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#transfer-event)
    
*   [Swap Event](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#swap-event)
    
*   [Bridge Event](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#bridge-event)
