*   [Error Details](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#error-details)
    

The following events are decoded in the GoldRush Streaming API:

*   [Transfer](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#transfer-event)
    
*   [Swap](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#swap-event)
    
*   [Bridge](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#bridge-event)
    
*   [Deposit](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#deposit-event)
    
*   [Withdraw](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#withdraw-event)
    
*   [Approve](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#approve-event)
    

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#transfer-event)

Transfer Event
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `from` | `string` | The source address |
| `to` | `string` | The destination address |
| `amount` | `string` | Unscaled token amount (scale by `metadata.contract_decimals`) |
| `quote_rate_usd` | `string` | Exchange rate of the token in USD |
| `quote_usd` | `string` | The quote amount of the token in USD |
| `contract_metadata` | `object` | Contract details including `contract_name`, `contract_address`, `contract_decimals`, and `contract_ticker_symbol` |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#swap-event)

Swap Event
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `token_in` | `string` | The input token address |
| `token_out` | `string` | The output token address |
| `amount_in` | `string` | The amount of input tokens |
| `amount_out` | `string` | The amount of output tokens |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#bridge-event)

Bridge Event
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `type` | `string` | The bridge transaction type |
| `typeString` | `string` | Human-readable bridge transaction type |
| `from` | `string` | The source address |
| `to` | `string` | The destination address |
| `amount` | `string` | Unscaled token amount (scale by `metadata.contract_decimals`) |
| `quote_rate_usd` | `string` | Exchange rate of the token in USD |
| `quote_usd` | `string` | The quote amount of the token in USD |
| `contract_metadata` | `object` | Contract details including `contract_name`, `contract_address`, `contract_decimals`, and `contract_ticker_symbol` |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#deposit-event)

Deposit Event
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `from` | `string` | The source address |
| `to` | `string` | The destination address |
| `amount` | `string` | Unscaled token amount (scale by `metadata.contract_decimals`) |
| `quote_rate_usd` | `string` | Exchange rate of the token in USD |
| `quote_usd` | `string` | The quote amount of the token in USD |
| `contract_metadata` | `object` | Contract details including `contract_name`, `contract_address`, `contract_decimals`, and `contract_ticker_symbol` |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#withdraw-event)

Withdraw Event
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `from` | `string` | The source address |
| `to` | `string` | The destination address |
| `amount` | `string` | Unscaled token amount (scale by `metadata.contract_decimals`) |
| `quote_rate_usd` | `string` | Exchange rate of the token in USD |
| `quote_usd` | `string` | The quote amount of the token in USD |
| `contract_metadata` | `object` | Contract details including `contract_name`, `contract_address`, `contract_decimals`, and `contract_ticker_symbol` |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#approve-event)

Approve Event
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `spender` | `string` | The address approved to spend tokens |
| `amount` | `string` | Unscaled token amount (scale by `metadata.contract_decimals`) |
| `quote_rate_usd` | `string` | Exchange rate of the token in USD |
| `quote_usd` | `string` | The quote amount of the token in USD |
| `contract_metadata` | `object` | Contract details including `contract_name`, `contract_address`, `contract_decimals`, and `contract_ticker_symbol` |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#transaction-logs)

Transaction Logs
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `emitter_address` | `string` | The address that emitted the log |
| `log_offset` | `integer` | The offset of the log in the transaction |
| `data` | `string` | The raw log data |
| `topics` | `array` | Array of log topics |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#error-details)

Error Details
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `message` | `string` | Error message describing what went wrong |

[GraphQL Endpoints](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/graphql-endpoints)
[GoldRush Playground](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-playground)

# Wallet Activity Stream - GoldRush API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/wallet-activity-stream#content-area)

[GoldRush API Documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=97917fde1507b0c14e79b83959fe1160)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=5bd4f921dcc81186bf369e7b33ec5734)](https://goldrush.dev/docs)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Available Streams

Wallet Activity Stream

[Overview](https://goldrush.dev/docs/overview)
[Foundational API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/overview)
[Streaming API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/overview)
[Chains](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/overview)

On this page

*   [Supported Actions](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/wallet-activity-stream#supported-actions)
    
*   [Parameters](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/wallet-activity-stream#parameters)
    
*   [Subscription](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/wallet-activity-stream#subscription)
    
*   [Basic Subscription Query](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/wallet-activity-stream#basic-subscription-query)
    
*   [Complete Subscription Query](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/wallet-activity-stream#complete-subscription-query)
    
*   [Response Format](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/wallet-activity-stream#response-format)
    
*   [Field Descriptions](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/wallet-activity-stream#field-descriptions)
    
*   [Decoded Events](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/wallet-activity-stream#decoded-events)
    

The Wallet Activity stream provides real-time updates on wallet **transactions, token transfers, and interactions with smart contracts** . This documentation follows our standard Streaming API structure.

Credit Cost
-----------

TBD

Supported Chains
----------------

*   `BASE_MAINNET`
*   `BASE_SEPOLIA`
*   `BASE_MAINNET_FLASHBLOCKS`
*   `BASE_SEPOLIA_FLASHBLOCKS`
*   `BSC_MAINNET`
*   `BSC_TESTNET`
*   `ETH_MAINNET`
*   `ETH_SEPOLIA`
*   `SONIC_MAINNET`
*   `HYPERCORE_MAINNET`
*   `MONAD_MAINNET`

**This stream is currently in Beta.** It is stable for testing and evaluation but may undergo changes in schema or behavior as we continue to improve it. **No API credits are currently charged.**We welcome your feedback so please [reach out](https://goldrush.dev/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#5a292f2a2a35282e1a39352c3b363f342e322b74393537)
 to us directly to report issues or request features.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/wallet-activity-stream#supported-actions)

Supported Actions
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

All transactions are returned as raw data, but the following transaction types are decoded:

*   [Transfer](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#transfer-event)
    
*   [Swap](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#swap-event)
    
*   [Bridge](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#bridge-event)
    
*   [Deposit](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#deposit-event)
    
*   [Withdraw](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#withdraw-event)
    
*   [Approve](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events#approve-event)
    

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/wallet-activity-stream#parameters)

Parameters
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `chain_name` | `enum` | Yes | Chain name to filter events (e.g. `BASE_MAINNET`, `ETH_MAINNET`, `BSC_MAINNET`) |
| `wallet_addresses` | `array<string>` | Yes | Addresses to track |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/wallet-activity-stream#subscription)

Subscription
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can subscribe to the `walletTxs` endpoint to receive events.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/wallet-activity-stream#basic-subscription-query)

Basic Subscription Query

Copy

Ask AI

    subscription {
      walletTxs(
        chain_name: BASE_MAINNET, 
        wallet_addresses: [\
            "0x4200000000000000000000000000000000000006",\
            "0x833589fCD6eDb6E08f4c7C32D4f71b54bdA02913"\
        ]) {
            block_signed_at
            block_height
            tx_hash
            tx_offset
            successful
            decoded_type        
      }
    }
    

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/wallet-activity-stream#complete-subscription-query)

Complete Subscription Query

Copy

Ask AI

    subscription {
      walletTxs(
        chain_name: BASE_MAINNET,
        wallet_addresses: [\
          "0x198ef79f1f515f02dfe9e3115ed9fc07183f02fc",\
          "0x4200000000000000000000000000000000000006"\
        ]
      ) {
        tx_hash
        from_address
        to_address
        value
        chain_name
        block_signed_at
        block_height
        block_hash
        miner_address
        gas_used
        tx_offset
        successful
        decoded_type
    
        decoded_details {
          ... on TransferTransaction {
            from
            to
            amount
            quote_usd
            quote_rate_usd
            contract_metadata {
              contract_name
              contract_address
              contract_decimals
              contract_ticker_symbol
            }
          }
          ... on SwapTransaction {
            token_in
            token_out
            amount_in
            amount_out
          }
          ... on BridgeTransaction {
            type
            typeString
            from
            to
            amount
            quote_usd
            quote_rate_usd
            contract_metadata {
              contract_name
              contract_address
              contract_decimals
              contract_ticker_symbol
            }
          }
          ... on DepositTransaction {
            from
            to
            amount
            quote_usd
            quote_rate_usd
            contract_metadata {
              contract_name
              contract_address
              contract_decimals
              contract_ticker_symbol
            }
          }
          ... on WithdrawTransaction {
            from
            to
            amount
            quote_usd
            quote_rate_usd
            contract_metadata {
              contract_name
              contract_address
              contract_decimals
              contract_ticker_symbol
            }
          }
          ... on ApproveTransaction {
            spender
            amount
            quote_usd
            quote_rate_usd
            contract_metadata {
              contract_name
              contract_address
              contract_decimals
              contract_ticker_symbol
            }
          }
          ... on ErrorDetails {
            message
          }
        }
    
        logs {
          emitter_address
          log_offset
          data
          topics
        }
      }
    }
    

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/wallet-activity-stream#response-format)

Here’s an example of the response data structure:

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/wallet-activity-stream#field-descriptions)

Field Descriptions

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `tx_hash` | `string` | The transaction hash |
| `from_address` | `string` | The sender’s address |
| `to_address` | `string` | The recipient’s address |
| `value` | `integer` | The transaction value in native currency |
| `chain_name` | `string` | The blockchain network where the transaction occurred |
| `block_signed_at` | `string` | ISO timestamp of when the block was signed |
| `block_height` | `integer` | The block number where the transaction was included |
| `block_hash` | `string` | The hash of the block containing the transaction |
| `miner_address` | `string` | The address of the block miner |
| `gas_used` | `integer` | The amount of gas used by the transaction |
| `tx_offset` | `integer` | The position of the transaction in the block |
| `successful` | `boolean` | Whether the transaction was successful |
| `decoded_type` | `string` | The type of decoded event (e.g., “SWAP”) |
| `decoded` | `object` | The decoded event data (varies by event type) |
| `logs` | `array` | Array of event logs emitted during the transaction |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/wallet-activity-stream#decoded-events)

Decoded Events
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Note from the [Complete Subscription Query](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/wallet-activity-stream#complete-subscription-query)
, this stream decodes events which you can fetch with fragment spreads. See the full schema of available [decoded events](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/decoded-events)
.

[Update Pairs Stream](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/update-pairs-stream)
[Get top trading wallets for token](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-token)

# Get PnL for wallet - GoldRush API Documentation

[Skip to main content](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-wallet#content-area)

[GoldRush API Documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=97917fde1507b0c14e79b83959fe1160)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/goldrush/6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA/logo/dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=6Ypq-wkqkJ_JUyHA&q=85&s=5bd4f921dcc81186bf369e7b33ec5734)](https://goldrush.dev/docs)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Available Queries

Get PnL for wallet

[Overview](https://goldrush.dev/docs/overview)
[Foundational API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/overview)
[Streaming API](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/overview)
[Chains](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/overview)

On this page

*   [Parameters](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-wallet#parameters)
    
*   [Query](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-wallet#query)
    
*   [Basic Query](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-wallet#basic-query)
    
*   [Complete Query](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-wallet#complete-query)
    
*   [Response Format](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-wallet#response-format)
    
*   [Field Descriptions](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-wallet#field-descriptions)
    
*   [GraphQL Playground](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-wallet#graphql-playground)
    

This GraphQL query provides detailed financial metrics, including unrealized and realized profit and loss (PnL), current balance, and transaction insights for each token held by a specific wallet address.

Credit Cost
-----------

TBD

Supported Chains
----------------

*   Base Mainnet
*   BSC Mainnet
*   Ethereum Mainnet
*   Gnosis Mainnet
*   Polygon Mainnet
*   Optimism Mainnet

**This query is currently in Beta.** It is stable for testing and evaluation but may undergo changes in schema or behavior as we continue to improve it. **No API credits are currently charged.**We welcome your feedback so please [reach out](https://goldrush.dev/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#31424441415e434571525e47505d545f4559401f525e5c)
 to us directly to report issues or request features.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-wallet#parameters)

Parameters
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Parameter | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `chain_name` | `enum` | Yes | Chain name to filter events (e.g., `BASE_MAINNET`, `ETH_MAINNET`, `BSC_MAINNET`) |
| `wallet_address` | `string` | Yes | The wallet address to query |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-wallet#query)

Query
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can query the `upnlForWallet` endpoint to retrieve detailed PnL metrics for a wallet.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-wallet#basic-query)

Basic Query

Copy

Ask AI

    query {
     upnlForToken(
        chain_name: ETH_MAINNET
        wallet_address: "0xfe97b0C517a84F98fc6eDe3CD26B43012d31992a"
      ) {
        token
        cost_basis
        current_price
        pnl_realized_usd
        pnl_unrealized_usd
        net_balance_change
      }
    }
    
    

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-wallet#complete-query)

Complete Query

Copy

Ask AI

    query{ 
    upnlForWallet(
        chain_name:ETH_MAINNET,
        wallet_address:"0xfe97b0C517a84F98fc6eDe3CD26B43012d31992a"
      ) {
        token
        cost_basis
        current_price
        pnl_realized_usd
        pnl_unrealized_usd
        net_balance_change
        marketcap_usd
        contract_metadata {
          contract_address
          contract_name
          contract_ticker_symbol
          contract_decimals
        }
      }
    }
    

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-wallet#response-format)

Response Format
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here’s an example of the response data structure:

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "data": {
        "upnlForWallet": [\
          {\
            "token": "0x7abc8a5768e6be61a6c693a6e4eacb5b60602c4d",\
            "cost_basis": 0.03219392,\
            "current_price": 0.032418,\
            "pnl_realized_usd": null,\
            "pnl_unrealized_usd": 318.22842,\
            "net_balance_change": 1420158,\
            "marketcap_usd": "32418001.4431",\
            "contract_metadata": {\
              "contract_address": "0x7abc8a5768e6be61a6c693a6e4eacb5b60602c4d",\
              "contract_name": "Covalent X Token",\
              "contract_ticker_symbol": "CXT",\
              "contract_decimals": 18\
            }\
          }\
        ]
      }
    }
    

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-wallet#field-descriptions)

Field Descriptions

| Field | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `token` | `string` | Token contract address, represented in uppercase with a 0x prefix |
| `cost_basis` | `float` | Simple Average cost basis per token in USD |
| `current_price` | `float` | Current market price per token in USD |
| `pnl_realized_usd` | `float` | Realized profit or loss in USD from completed trades |
| `pnl_unrealized_usd` | `float` | Current unrealized profit or loss in USD based on the latest price |
| `net_balance_change` | `BigInteger` | Net token movement (inflow minus outflow) over the past 7 days |
| `marketcap_usd` | `string` | Token’s estimated market capitalization in USD |
| `contract_metadata` | `object` | Contains metadata details for the token contract |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/upnl-for-wallet#graphql-playground)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

GraphQL Endpoints

On this page

*   [List of endpoints](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/graphql-endpoints#list-of-endpoints)
    
*   [Fetching the schema](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/graphql-endpoints#fetching-the-schema)
    

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/graphql-endpoints#list-of-endpoints)

List of endpoints
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Functionality | Endpoint Type |     |
| --- | --- | --- |
| New DEX Pairs Stream | `subscription` | `subscription { newPairs { ... } }` |
| Wallet ActivityStream | `subscription` | `subscription { walletTxs { ... } }` |
| OHLC Pairs Stream | `subscription` | `subscription { ohlcvCandlesForPair { ... } }` |
| OHLC Tokens Stream | `subscription` | `subscription { ohlcvCandlesForToken { ... } }` |
| Get top trading wallets for token | `query` | `query { upnlForToken { ... } }` |
| Get PnL for wallet | `query` | `query { upnlForWallet { ... } }` |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/graphql-endpoints#fetching-the-schema)

Fetching the schema
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

Ask AI

    query IntrospectionQuery {
      __schema {
        queryType {
          name
        }
        mutationType {
          name
        }
        subscriptionType {
          name
        }
        types {
          ...FullType
        }
        directives {
          name
          description
    
          locations
          args {
            ...InputValue
          }
        }
      }
    }
    
    fragment FullType on __Type {
      kind
      name
      description
    
      fields(includeDeprecated: true) {
        name
        description
        args {
          ...InputValue
        }
        type {
          ...TypeRef
        }
        isDeprecated
        deprecationReason
      }
      inputFields {
        ...InputValue
      }
      interfaces {
        ...TypeRef
      }
      enumValues(includeDeprecated: true) {
        name
        description
        isDeprecated
        deprecationReason
      }
      possibleTypes {
        ...TypeRef
      }
    }
    
    fragment InputValue on __InputValue {
      name
      description
      type {
        ...TypeRef
      }
      defaultValue
    }
    
    fragment TypeRef on __Type {
      kind
      name
      ofType {
        kind
        name
        ofType {
          kind
          name
          ofType {
            kind
            name
            ofType {
              kind
              name
              ofType {
                kind
                name
                ofType {
                  kind
                  name
                  ofType {
                    kind
                    name
                    ofType {
                      kind
                      name
                      ofType {
                        kind
                        name
                      }
                    }
                  }
                }
              }
            }
          }
        }
      }
    }

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/monad#overview)

Overview
----------------------------------------------------------------

GoldRush offers the most comprehensive Monad Data API suite for developers, analysts, and enterprises. Whether you’re building a DeFi dashboard, a wallet, a trading bot, an AI agent or a compliance platform, our Monad Data APIs provide fast, accurate, and developer-friendly access to the essential onchain data you need.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/monad#supported-apis)

Supported APIs

[Foundational API\
----------------\
\
Access structured historical blockchain data across 100+ chains using REST APIs. Get token balances, transaction histories, decoded event logs, NFT assets, token holders and more.  \
  \
**Use cases: Wallets, portfolio trackers, crypto accounting & tax tools, and DeFi dashboards.**\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api)
[Streaming API\
-------------\
\
Subscribe to real-time blockchain events with sub-second latency using GraphQL over WebSockets. Track token transfers, DEX activity, wallet movements, and OHLCV candlestick data across fast chains like Base and Solana.  \
  \
**Use cases: Trading bots & dashboards, gaming, and AI Agents.**\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/monad#mainnet)

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/monad#sdk-usage)

SDK Usage

TypeScript SDK (Mainnet)

TypeScript SDK (Monad Testnet)

Copy

Ask AI

    import { GoldRushClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    const client = new GoldRushClient("API_KEY");
    const resp = await client.BalanceService.getTokenBalancesForWalletAddress({
        chainName: "monad-mainnet",
        walletAddress: "0xd8dA6BF26964aF9D7eEd9e03E53415D37aA96045"
    });

Overview
-----------------------------------------------------------------

GoldRush offers the most comprehensive Plasma Data API suite for developers, analysts, and enterprises. Whether you’re building a DeFi dashboard, a wallet, a trading bot, an AI agent or a compliance platform, our Plasma Data APIs provide fast, accurate, and developer-friendly access to the essential onchain data you need.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/plasma#supported-apis)

Supported APIs

[Foundational API\
----------------\
\
Access structured historical blockchain data across 100+ chains using REST APIs. Get token balances, transaction histories, decoded event logs, NFT assets, token holders and more.  \
  \
**Use cases: Wallets, portfolio trackers, crypto accounting & tax tools, and DeFi dashboards.**\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/plasma#mainnet)

Supported APIs

[Streaming API\
-------------\
\
Subscribe to real-time blockchain events with sub-second latency using GraphQL over WebSockets. Track token transfers, DEX activity, wallet movements, and OHLCV candlestick data across fast chains like Base and Solana.  \
  \
**Use cases: Trading bots & dashboards, gaming, and AI Agents.**\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/harmony#overview)

Overview
------------------------------------------------------------------

GoldRush offers the most comprehensive Harmony Data API suite for developers, analysts, and enterprises. Whether you’re building a DeFi dashboard, a wallet, a trading bot, an AI agent or a compliance platform, our Harmony Data APIs provide fast, accurate, and developer-friendly access to the essential onchain data you need.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/harmony#supported-apis)

Supported APIs

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/harmony#mainnet)

Mainnet
----------------------------------------------------------------

| **Property** | **Value** |
| --- | --- |
| **Chain Name** | `harmony-mainnet` |
| **Chain ID** | `1666600000` |
| **Network Type** | Archived Chain |
| **Support Level** | archived |
| **Block Explorer** | [Explorer](https://explorer.harmony.one/) |
| **Official Website** | [Harmony Website](https://www.harmony.one/) |
| **Native Gas Token** | ONE |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/harmony#testnet)

Testnet
----------------------------------------------------------------

| **Property** | **Value** |
| --- | --- |
| **Chain Name** | `harmony-testnet` |
| **Chain ID** | `1666700000` |
| **Purpose** | Development and testing network |
| **Support Level** | archived |
| **Block Explorer** | [Explorer](https://explorer.testnet.harmony.one/) |
| **Official Website** | [Harmony Testnet Website](https://www.harmony.one/) |
| **Native Gas Token** | ONE |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/harmony#api-usage)

API Usage
--------------------------------------------------------------------

To use this blockchain network in GoldRush API calls, use:

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/harmony#chain-name)

Chain Name

*   `harmony-mainnet` (mainnet)
*   `harmony-testnet` (testnet)

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/harmony#example-api-calls)

Example API Calls

Chain Name (Mainnet)

Chain Name (Harmony Testnet)

Copy

Ask AI

    curl -X GET "https://api.covalenthq.com/v1/harmony-mainnet/address/0xd8dA6BF26964aF9D7eEd9e03E53415D37aA96045/balances_v2/?key=API_KEY"
    

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/harmony#sdk-usage)

SDK Usage

TypeScript SDK (Mainnet)

TypeScript SDK (Harmony Testnet)

Copy

Ask AI

    import { GoldRushClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    const client = new GoldRushClient("API_KEY");
    const resp = await client.BalanceService.getTokenBalancesForWalletAddress({
        chainName: "harmony-mainnet",
        walletAddress: "0xd8dA6BF26964aF9D7eEd9e03E53415D37aA96045"
    });

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/sonic#overview)

Overview
----------------------------------------------------------------

GoldRush offers the most comprehensive Sonic Data API suite for developers, analysts, and enterprises. Whether you’re building a DeFi dashboard, a wallet, a trading bot, an AI agent or a compliance platform, our Sonic Data APIs provide fast, accurate, and developer-friendly access to the essential onchain data you need.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/sonic#supported-apis)

Supported APIs

[Foundational API\
----------------\
\
Access structured historical blockchain data across 100+ chains using REST APIs. Get token balances, transaction histories, decoded event logs, NFT assets, token holders and more.  \
  \
**Use cases: Wallets, portfolio trackers, crypto accounting & tax tools, and DeFi dashboards.**\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api)
[Streaming API\
-------------\
\
Subscribe to real-time blockchain events with sub-second latency using GraphQL over WebSockets. Track token transfers, DEX activity, wallet movements, and OHLCV candlestick data across fast chains like Base and Solana.  \
  \
**Use cases: Trading bots & dashboards, gaming, and AI Agents.**\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/sonic#mainnet)

Mainnet
--------------------------------------------------------------

| **Property** | **Value** |
| --- | --- |
| **Chain Name** | `sonic-mainnet` |
| **Chain ID** | `146` |
| **Network Type** | Frontier Chain |
| **Support Level** | frontier |
| **Block Explorer** | [Sonic Explorer](https://sonicscan.org/) |
| **Official Website** | [Sonic Website](https://www.soniclabs.com/) |
| **Native Gas Token** | S   |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/sonic#api-usage)

------------------------------------------------------------------

####

####

Example API Calls

Chain Name (Mainnet)

Copy

Ask AI

    curl -X GET "https://api.covalenthq.com/v1/sonic-mainnet/address/0xd8dA6BF26964aF9D7eEd9e03E53415D37aA96045/balances_v2/?key=API_KEY"
    

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/sonic#sdk-usage)

SDK Usage

TypeScript SDK (Mainnet)

Copy

Ask AI

    import { GoldRushClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    const client = new GoldRushClient("API_KEY");
    const resp = await client.BalanceService.getTokenBalancesForWalletAddress({
        chainName: "sonic-mainnet",
        walletAddress: "0xd8dA6BF26964aF9D7eEd9e03E53415D37aA96045"
    });
    

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/sonic#foundational-api-support)

Foundational API Support
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This chain supports **22** GoldRush Foundational APIs:

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/sonic#wallet-api)

Wallet API

*   **[Get token balances for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-balances-for-address)
    **
*   **[Get native token balance for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-native-token-balance)
    **
*   **[Get historical portfolio value over time](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-portfolio-value-over-time)
    **
*   **[Get ERC20 token transfers for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address)
    **

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/sonic#pricing-api)

Pricing API

*   **[Get historical token prices](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-historical-token-prices)
    **

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/sonic#security-api)

Security API

*   **[Get token approvals for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/security/get-token-approvals-for-address)
    **

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/sonic#activity-feed-api)

Activity Feed API

*   **[Get a transaction](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-a-transaction)
    **
*   **[Get transaction summary for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-transaction-summary-for-address)
    **
*   **[Get earliest transactions for address (v3)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-earliest-transactions-for-address-v3)
    **
*   **[Get recent transactions for address (v3)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-recent-transactions-for-address-v3)
    **
*   **[Get paginated transactions for address (v3)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-paginated-transactions-for-address-v3)
    **
*   **[Get bulk time bucket transactions for address (v3)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-time-bucket-transactions-for-address-v3)
    **
*   **[Get all transactions in a block (v3)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block)
    **
*   **[Get all transactions in a block by page (v3)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block-by-page)
    **

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/sonic#block-explorer-api)

Block Explorer API

*   **[Get a block](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-a-block)
    **
*   **[Get all chain statuses](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-all-chain-statuses)
    **
*   **[Get all chains](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-all-chains)
    **
*   **[Get block heights](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-block-heights)
    **
*   **[Get gas prices](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-gas-prices)
    **
*   **[Get log events by contract address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-contract-address)
    **
*   **[Get log events by topic hash(es)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash)
    **
*   **[Get logs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-logs)
    **

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/sonic#streaming-api-support)

Streaming API Support
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This chain supports the following GoldRush Streaming APIs:

*   [New DEX Pairs Stream](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/new-dex-pairs-stream)
    
*   [OHLCV Pairs Stream](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-pairs-stream)
    
*   [OHLCV Tokens Stream](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-tokens-stream)
    
*   [Update Pairs Stream](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/update-pairs-stream)
    
*   [Wallet Activity Stream](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/wallet-activity-stream)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/solana#overview)

Overview
-----------------------------------------------------------------

GoldRush offers the most comprehensive Solana Data API suite for developers, analysts, and enterprises. Whether you’re building a DeFi dashboard, a wallet, a trading bot, an AI agent or a compliance platform, our Solana Data APIs provide fast, accurate, and developer-friendly access to the essential onchain data you need.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/solana#supported-apis)

Supported APIs

[Foundational API\
----------------\
\
Access structured spot data such as token balances.Use cases: Wallets, portfolio trackers\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api)
[Streaming API\
-------------\
\
Subscribe to real-time blockchain events with sub-second latency using GraphQL over WebSockets. Track token transfers, DEX activity, wallet movements, and OHLCV candlestick data across fast chains like Base and Solana.  \
  \
**Use cases: Trading bots & dashboards, gaming, and AI Agents.**\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/solana#mainnet)

| --- | --- |
| **Chain Name** | `solana-mainnet` |
| **Chain ID** | `1399811149` |
| **Network Type** | Frontier Chain |
| **Support Level** | frontier |
| **Block Explorer** | [Explorer](https://explorer.solana.com/) |
| **Official Website** | [Solana Website](https://solana.com/) |
| **Native Gas Token** | SOL |

Chain Name (Mainnet)

Ask AI

SDK Usage

TypeScript SDK (Mainnet)

Copy

Ask AI

    import { GoldRushClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    const client = new GoldRushClient("API_KEY");
    const resp = await client.BalanceService.getTokenBalancesForWalletAddress({
        chainName: "solana-mainnet",
        walletAddress: "4ZJhPQAgUseCsWhKvJLTmmRRUV74fdoTpQLNfKoekbPY"
    });

Overview
---------------------------------------------------------------

GoldRush offers the most comprehensive Lisk Data API suite for developers, analysts, and enterprises. Whether you’re building a DeFi dashboard, a wallet, a trading bot, an AI agent or a compliance platform, our Lisk Data APIs provide fast, accurate, and developer-friendly access to the essential onchain data you need.

Overview
-------------------------------------------------------------------

GoldRush offers the most comprehensive Optimism Data API suite for developers, analysts, and enterprises. Whether you’re building a DeFi dashboard, a wallet, a trading bot, an AI agent or a compliance platform, our Optimism Data APIs provide fast, accurate, and developer-friendly access to the essential onchain data you need.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/optimism#supported-apis)

Supported APIs

[Foundational API\
----------------\
\
Access structured historical blockchain data across 100+ chains using REST APIs. Get token balances, transaction histories, decoded event logs, NFT assets, token holders and more.  \
  \
**Use cases: Wallets, portfolio trackers, crypto accounting & tax tools, and DeFi dashboards.**\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/optimism#mainnet)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/ethereum#overview)

Overview
-------------------------------------------------------------------

GoldRush offers the most comprehensive Ethereum Data API suite for developers, analysts, and enterprises. Whether you’re building a DeFi dashboard, a wallet, a trading bot, an AI agent or a compliance platform, our Ethereum Data APIs provide fast, accurate, and developer-friendly access to the essential onchain data you need.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/ethereum#supported-apis)

Supported APIs

[Foundational API\
----------------\
\
Access structured historical blockchain data across 100+ chains using REST APIs. Get token balances, transaction histories, decoded event logs, NFT assets, token holders and more.  \
  \
**Use cases: Wallets, portfolio trackers, crypto accounting & tax tools, and DeFi dashboards.**\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api)
[Streaming API\
-------------\
\
Subscribe to real-time blockchain events with sub-second latency using GraphQL over WebSockets. Track token transfers, DEX activity, wallet movements, and OHLCV candlestick data across fast chains like Base and Solana.  \
  \
**Use cases: Trading bots & dashboards, gaming, and AI Agents.**\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/ethereum#mainnet)

Mainnet
-----------------------------------------------------------------

| **Property** | **Value** |
| --- | --- |
| **Chain Name** | `eth-mainnet` |
| **Chain ID** | `1` |
| **Network Type** | Foundational Chain |
| **Support Level** | foundational |
| **Block Explorer** | [Etherscan](https://etherscan.io/) |
| **Official Website** | [Ethereum Website](https://ethereum.org/) |
| **Native Gas Token** | ETH |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/ethereum#testnets)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/ethereum#api-usage)

API Usage
---------------------------------------------------------------------

To use this blockchain network in GoldRush API calls, use:

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/ethereum#chain-name)

Chain Name

*   `eth-mainnet` (mainnet)
*   `eth-holesky` (testnet)
*   `eth-sepolia` (testnet)

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/ethereum#example-api-calls)

Example API Calls

Chain Name (Mainnet)

Chain Name (Holesky Testnet)

Chain Name (Ethereum Sepolia Testnet)

Copy

Ask AI

    curl -X GET "https://api.covalenthq.com/v1/eth-mainnet/address/0xd8dA6BF26964aF9D7eEd9e03E53415D37aA96045/balances_v2/?key=API_KEY"
    

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/ethereum#sdk-usage)

SDK Usage

TypeScript SDK (Mainnet)

TypeScript SDK (Holesky Testnet)

TypeScript SDK (Ethereum Sepolia Testnet)

Copy

Ask AI

    import { GoldRushClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    const client = new GoldRushClient("API_KEY");
    const resp = await client.BalanceService.getTokenBalancesForWalletAddress({
        chainName: "eth-mainnet",
        walletAddress: "0xd8dA6BF26964aF9D7eEd9e03E53415D37aA96045"
    });
    

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/ethereum#foundational-api-support)

Foundational API Support
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This chain supports **28** GoldRush Foundational APIs:

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/ethereum#wallet-api)

Wallet API

*   **[Get token holders as of any block height (v2)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-holders-as-of-any-block-height-v2)
    **
*   **[Get historical token balances for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address)
    **
*   **[Get token balances for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-balances-for-address)
    **
*   **[Get native token balance for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-native-token-balance)
    **
*   **[Get historical portfolio value over time](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-portfolio-value-over-time)
    **
*   **[Get ERC20 token transfers for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address)
    **

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/ethereum#nft-api)

NFT API

*   **[Get NFTs for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/get-nfts-for-address)
    **
*   **[Check ownership in NFT collection](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/check-ownership-in-nft-collection)
    **
*   **[Check ownership in NFT collection for specific token](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/check-ownership-in-nft-collection-token)
    **

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/ethereum#pricing-api)

Pricing API

*   **[Get pool spot prices](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-pool-spot-prices)
    **
*   **[Get historical token prices](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-historical-token-prices)
    **

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/ethereum#security-api)

Security API

    **

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/ethereum#activity-feed-api)

Activity Feed API

*   **[Get a transaction](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-a-transaction)
    **
*   **[Get transaction summary for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-transaction-summary-for-address)
    **
*   **[Get earliest transactions for address (v3)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-earliest-transactions-for-address-v3)
    **
*   **[Get recent transactions for address (v3)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-recent-transactions-for-address-v3)
    **
*   **[Get paginated transactions for address (v3)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-paginated-transactions-for-address-v3)
    **
*   **[Get bulk time bucket transactions for address (v3)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-time-bucket-transactions-for-address-v3)
    **
*   **[Get all transactions in a block (v3)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block)
    **
*   **[Get all transactions in a block by page (v3)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block-by-page)
    **

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/ethereum#block-explorer-api)

Block Explorer API

*   **[Get a block](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-a-block)
    **
*   **[Get all chain statuses](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-all-chain-statuses)
    **
*   **[Get all chains](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-all-chains)
    **

    **

Streaming API Support
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This chain supports the following GoldRush Streaming APIs:

*   [New DEX Pairs Stream](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/new-dex-pairs-stream)
    
*   [OHLCV Pairs Stream](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-pairs-stream)
    
*   [OHLCV Tokens Stream](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/ohlcv-tokens-stream)
    
*   [Update Pairs Stream](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/update-pairs-stream)
    
*   [Wallet Activity Stream](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api/wallet-activity-stream)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/bnb-smart-chain-bsc#overview)

Overview
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

GoldRush offers the most comprehensive BNB Smart Chain (BSC) Data API suite for developers, analysts, and enterprises. Whether you’re building a DeFi dashboard, a wallet, a trading bot, an AI agent or a compliance platform, our BNB Smart Chain (BSC) Data APIs provide fast, accurate, and developer-friendly access to the essential onchain data you need.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/bnb-smart-chain-bsc#supported-apis)

Supported APIs

[Foundational API\
----------------\
\
Access structured historical blockchain data across 100+ chains using REST APIs. Get token balances, transaction histories, decoded event logs, NFT assets, token holders and more.  \
  \
**Use cases: Wallets, portfolio trackers, crypto accounting & tax tools, and DeFi dashboards.**\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api)
[Streaming API\
-------------\
\
Subscribe to real-time blockchain events with sub-second latency using GraphQL over WebSockets. Track token transfers, DEX activity, wallet movements, and OHLCV candlestick data across fast chains like Base and Solana.  \
  \
**Use cases: Trading bots & dashboards, gaming, and AI Agents.**\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/bnb-smart-chain-bsc#mainnet)

| **Chain Name** | `bsc-mainnet` |
| **Chain ID** | `56` |
| **Network Type** | Foundational Chain |
| **Support Level** | foundational |
| **Block Explorer** | [BscScan](https://bscscan.com/) |
| **Official Website** | [BNB Smart Chain (BSC) Website](https://www.bnbchain.org/en) |
| **Native Gas Token** | BNB |

Overview
----------------------------------------------------------------------------

GoldRush offers the most comprehensive Avalanche C-Chain Data API suite for developers, analysts, and enterprises. Whether you’re building a DeFi dashboard, a wallet, a trading bot, an AI agent or a compliance platform, our Avalanche C-Chain Data APIs provide fast, accurate, and developer-friendly access to the essential onchain data you need.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/avalanche-c-chain#supported-apis)

Supported APIs

[Foundational API\
----------------\
\
Access structured historical blockchain data across 100+ chains using REST APIs. Get token balances, transaction histories, decoded event logs, NFT assets, token holders and more.  \
  \
**Use cases: Wallets, portfolio trackers, crypto accounting & tax tools, and DeFi dashboards.**\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/avalanche-c-chain#mainnet)

| **Support Level** | frontier |
| **Block Explorer** | [Explorer](https://avascan.info/blockchain/c/) |
| **Official Website** | [Avalanche C-Chain Website](https://www.avax.network/) |

Chain Name (Avalanche Fuji Testnet)

Copy

Ask AI

SDK Usage

TypeScript SDK (Mainnet)

TypeScript SDK (Avalanche Fuji Testnet)

Copy

Ask AI

    import { GoldRushClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    const client = new GoldRushClient("API_KEY");
    const resp = await client.BalanceService.getTokenBalancesForWalletAddress({
        chainName: "avalanche-mainnet",
        walletAddress: "0xd8dA6BF26964aF9D7eEd9e03E53415D37aA96045"
    });

Overview
---------------------------------------------------------------------

GoldRush offers the most comprehensive Axie/Ronin Data API suite for developers, analysts, and enterprises. Whether you’re building a DeFi dashboard, a wallet, a trading bot, an AI agent or a compliance platform, our Axie/Ronin Data APIs provide fast, accurate, and developer-friendly access to the essential onchain data you need.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/axie-ronin#supported-apis)

Supported APIs

[Foundational API\
----------------\
\
Access structured historical blockchain data across 100+ chains using REST APIs. Get token balances, transaction histories, decoded event logs, NFT assets, token holders and more.  \
  \
**Use cases: Wallets, portfolio trackers, crypto accounting & tax tools, and DeFi dashboards.**\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api)

SDK Usage

TypeScript SDK (Mainnet)

Copy

Ask AI

    import { GoldRushClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    const client = new GoldRushClient("API_KEY");
    const resp = await client.BalanceService.getTokenBalancesForWalletAddress({
        chainName: "axie-mainnet",
        walletAddress: "0xd8dA6BF26964aF9D7eEd9e03E53415D37aA96045"
    });

Overview
-------------------------------------------------------------------

GoldRush offers the most comprehensive ApeChain Data API suite for developers, analysts, and enterprises. Whether you’re building a DeFi dashboard, a wallet, a trading bot, an AI agent or a compliance platform, our ApeChain Data APIs provide fast, accurate, and developer-friendly access to the essential onchain data you need.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/apechain#supported-apis)

Supported APIs

[Foundational API\
----------------\
\
Access structured historical blockchain data across 100+ chains using REST APIs. Get token balances, transaction histories, decoded event logs, NFT assets, token holders and more.  \
  \
**Use cases: Wallets, portfolio trackers, crypto accounting & tax tools, and DeFi dashboards.**\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/apechain#mainnet)

Mainnet
-----------------------------------------------------------------

| **Property** | **Value** |
| --- | --- |
| **Chain Name** | `apechain-mainnet` |
| **Chain ID** | `33139` |
| **Network Type** | Frontier Chain |
| **Support Level** | frontier |
| **Block Explorer** | [ApeChain Explorer](https://apechain.calderaexplorer.xyz/) |
| **Official Website** | [ApeChain Website](https://apechain.com/) |
| **Native Gas Token** | APE |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/apechain#api-usage)

API Usage
---------------------------------------------------------------------

To use this blockchain network in GoldRush API calls, use:

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/apechain#chain-name)

Chain Name

*   `apechain-mainnet` (mainnet)

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/apechain#example-api-calls)

Example API Calls

Chain Name (Mainnet)

Copy

Ask AI

    curl -X GET "https://api.covalenthq.com/v1/apechain-mainnet/address/0xd8dA6BF26964aF9D7eEd9e03E53415D37aA96045/balances_v2/?key=API_KEY"
    

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/apechain#sdk-usage)

SDK Usage

TypeScript SDK (Mainnet)

Copy

Ask AI

    import { GoldRushClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    const client = new GoldRushClient("API_KEY");
    const resp = await client.BalanceService.getTokenBalancesForWalletAddress({
        chainName: "apechain-mainnet",
        walletAddress: "0xd8dA6BF26964aF9D7eEd9e03E53415D37aA96045"
    });

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/mantle#overview)

Overview
-----------------------------------------------------------------

GoldRush offers the most comprehensive Mantle Data API suite for developers, analysts, and enterprises. Whether you’re building a DeFi dashboard, a wallet, a trading bot, an AI agent or a compliance platform, our Mantle Data APIs provide fast, accurate, and developer-friendly access to the essential onchain data you need.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/mantle#supported-apis)

Supported APIs

[Foundational API\
----------------\
\
Access structured historical blockchain data across 100+ chains using REST APIs. Get token balances, transaction histories, decoded event logs, NFT assets, token holders and more.  \
  \
**Use cases: Wallets, portfolio trackers, crypto accounting & tax tools, and DeFi dashboards.**\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/mantle#mainnet)

Mainnet
---------------------------------------------------------------

| **Property** | **Value** |
| --- | --- |
| **Chain Name** | `mantle-mainnet` |
| **Chain ID** | `5000` |
| **Network Type** | Frontier Chain |
| **Support Level** | frontier |
| **Block Explorer** | [Explorer](https://explorer.mantle.xyz/) |
| **Official Website** | [Mantle Website](https://www.mantle.xyz/) |
| **Native Gas Token** | MNT |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/mantle#api-usage)

API Usage
-------------------------------------------------------------------

To use this blockchain network in GoldRush API calls, use:

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/mantle#chain-name)

Chain Name

*   `mantle-mainnet` (mainnet)

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/mantle#example-api-calls)

Example API Calls

Chain Name (Mainnet)

Copy

Ask AI

    curl -X GET "https://api.covalenthq.com/v1/mantle-mainnet/address/0xd8dA6BF26964aF9D7eEd9e03E53415D37aA96045/balances_v2/?key=API_KEY"
    

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/mantle#sdk-usage)

SDK Usage

TypeScript SDK (Mainnet)

Copy

Ask AI

    import { GoldRushClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    const client = new GoldRushClient("API_KEY");
    const resp = await client.BalanceService.getTokenBalancesForWalletAddress({
        chainName: "mantle-mainnet",
        walletAddress: "0xd8dA6BF26964aF9D7eEd9e03E53415D37aA96045"
    });
    

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/mantle#foundational-api-support)

Foundational API Support
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This chain supports **23** GoldRush Foundational APIs:

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/mantle#wallet-api)

Wallet API

*   **[Get token balances for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-balances-for-address)
    **
*   **[Get native token balance for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-native-token-balance)
    **
*   **[Get historical portfolio value over time](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-portfolio-value-over-time)
    **
*   **[Get ERC20 token transfers for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address)
    **

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/mantle#nft-api)

NFT API

*   **[Get NFTs for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/get-nfts-for-address)
    **

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/mantle#pricing-api)

Pricing API

*   **[Get historical token prices](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-historical-token-prices)
    **

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/mantle#security-api)

Security API

*   **[Get token approvals for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/security/get-token-approvals-for-address)
    **

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/mantle#activity-feed-api)

Activity Feed API

*   **[Get a transaction](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-a-transaction)
    **
*   **[Get transaction summary for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-transaction-summary-for-address)
    **
*   **[Get earliest transactions for address (v3)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-earliest-transactions-for-address-v3)
    **
*   **[Get recent transactions for address (v3)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-recent-transactions-for-address-v3)
    **
*   **[Get paginated transactions for address (v3)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-paginated-transactions-for-address-v3)
    **
*   **[Get bulk time bucket transactions for address (v3)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-time-bucket-transactions-for-address-v3)
    **
*   **[Get all transactions in a block (v3)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block)
    **
*   **[Get all transactions in a block by page (v3)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block-by-page)
    **

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/mantle#block-explorer-api)

Block Explorer API

*   **[Get a block](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-a-block)
    **
*   **[Get all chain statuses](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-all-chain-statuses)
    **
*   **[Get all chains](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-all-chains)
    **
*   **[Get block heights](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-block-heights)
    **
*   **[Get gas prices](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-gas-prices)
    **
*   **[Get log events by contract address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-contract-address)
    **
*   **[Get log events by topic hash(es)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash)
    **
*   **[Get logs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-logs)
    **

Overview

Whether you’re building a DeFi dashboard, a wallet, a trading bot, an AI agent or a compliance platform, our Sei Data APIs provide fast, accurate, and developer-friendly access to the essential onchain data you need.

  \

Whether you’re building a DeFi dashboard, a wallet, a trading bot, an AI agent or a compliance platform, our Blast Data APIs provide fast, accurate, and developer-friendly access to the essential onchain data you need.

Overview
----------------------------------------------------------------

GoldRush offers the most comprehensive Taiko Data API suite for developers, analysts, and enterprises. Whether you’re building a DeFi dashboard, a wallet, a trading bot, an AI agent or a compliance platform, our Taiko Data APIs provide fast, accurate, and developer-friendly access to the essential onchain data you need.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/taiko#supported-apis)

Supported APIs

[Foundational API\
----------------\
\
Access structured historical blockchain data across 100+ chains using REST APIs. Get token balances, transaction histories, decoded event logs, NFT assets, token holders and more.  \
  \
**Use cases: Wallets, portfolio trackers, crypto accounting & tax tools, and DeFi dashboards.**\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api)

Chain Name (Mainnet)

Copy

Ask AI

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/taiko#sdk-usage)

SDK Usage

TypeScript SDK (Mainnet)

Copy

Ask AI

    import { GoldRushClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    const client = new GoldRushClient("API_KEY");
    const resp = await client.BalanceService.getTokenBalancesForWalletAddress({
        chainName: "taiko-mainnet",
        walletAddress: "0xd8dA6BF26964aF9D7eEd9e03E53415D37aA96045"
    });

    const client = new GoldRushClient("API_KEY");
    const resp = await client.BalanceService.getTokenBalancesForWalletAddress({
        chainName: "covalent-internal-network-v1",
        walletAddress: "0xd8dA6BF26964aF9D7eEd9e03E53415D37aA96045"
    });

Overview
--------------------------------------------------------------

GoldRush offers the most comprehensive Ink Data API suite for developers, analysts, and enterprises. Whether you’re building a DeFi dashboard, a wallet, a trading bot, an AI agent or a compliance platform, our Ink Data APIs provide fast, accurate, and developer-friendly access to the essential onchain data you need.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/ink#supported-apis)

Supported APIs

[Foundational API\
----------------\
\
Access structured historical blockchain data across 100+ chains using REST APIs. Get token balances, transaction histories, decoded event logs, NFT assets, token holders and more.  \
  \
**Use cases: Wallets, portfolio trackers, crypto accounting & tax tools, and DeFi dashboards.**\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/oasis-sapphire#overview)

Overview
-------------------------------------------------------------------------

GoldRush offers the most comprehensive Oasis Sapphire Data API suite for developers, analysts, and enterprises. Whether you’re building a DeFi dashboard, a wallet, a trading bot, an AI agent or a compliance platform, our Oasis Sapphire Data APIs provide fast, accurate, and developer-friendly access to the essential onchain data you need.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/oasis-sapphire#supported-apis)

Supported APIs

[Foundational API\
----------------\
\
Access structured historical blockchain data across 100+ chains using REST APIs. Get token balances, transaction histories, decoded event logs, NFT assets, token holders and more.  \
  \
**Use cases: Wallets, portfolio trackers, crypto accounting & tax tools, and DeFi dashboards.**\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/oasis-sapphire#mainnet)

Mainnet
-----------------------------------------------------------------------

| **Property** | **Value** |
| --- | --- |
| **Chain Name** | `oasis-sapphire-mainnet` |
| **Chain ID** | `23294` |
| **Network Type** | Frontier Chain |
| **Support Level** | frontier |
| **Block Explorer** | [Explorer](https://explorer.sapphire.oasis.io/) |
| **Official Website** | [Oasis Sapphire Website](https://docs.oasis.io/dapp/sapphire/) |
| **Native Gas Token** | ROSE |

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/oasis-sapphire#api-usage)

API Usage
---------------------------------------------------------------------------

To use this blockchain network in GoldRush API calls, use:

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/oasis-sapphire#chain-name)

Chain Name

*   `oasis-sapphire-mainnet` (mainnet)

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/oasis-sapphire#example-api-calls)

Example API Calls

Chain Name (Mainnet)

Copy

Ask AI

    curl -X GET "https://api.covalenthq.com/v1/oasis-sapphire-mainnet/address/0xd8dA6BF26964aF9D7eEd9e03E53415D37aA96045/balances_v2/?key=API_KEY"
    

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/oasis-sapphire#sdk-usage)

SDK Usage

TypeScript SDK (Mainnet)

Copy

Ask AI

    import { GoldRushClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    const client = new GoldRushClient("API_KEY");
    const resp = await client.BalanceService.getTokenBalancesForWalletAddress({
        chainName: "oasis-sapphire-mainnet",
        walletAddress: "0xd8dA6BF26964aF9D7eEd9e03E53415D37aA96045"
    });
    

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/oasis-sapphire#foundational-api-support)

Foundational API Support
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

####

Wallet API

*   **[Get token balances for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-balances-for-address)
    **

    **
*   **[Get historical portfolio value over time](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-portfolio-value-over-time)
    **
*   **[Get ERC20 token transfers for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address)
    **

Activity Feed API

*   **[Get a transaction](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-a-transaction)
    **
*   **[Get transaction summary for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-transaction-summary-for-address)
    **
*   **[Get earliest transactions for address (v3)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-earliest-transactions-for-address-v3)
    **
*   **[Get recent transactions for address (v3)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-recent-transactions-for-address-v3)
    **
*   **[Get paginated transactions for address (v3)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-paginated-transactions-for-address-v3)
    **
*   **[Get bulk time bucket transactions for address (v3)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-time-bucket-transactions-for-address-v3)
    **
*   **[Get all transactions in a block (v3)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block)
    **
*   **[Get all transactions in a block by page (v3)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block-by-page)
    **

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/oasis-sapphire#block-explorer-api)

*   **[Get a block](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-a-block)
    **

    **

    **
*   **[Get block heights](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-block-heights)
    **
*   **[Get gas prices](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-gas-prices)
    **
*   **[Get log events by contract address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-contract-address)
    **
*   **[Get log events by topic hash(es)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash)
    **
*   **[Get logs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-logs)
    **

Overview
-------------------------------------------------------------------

GoldRush offers the most comprehensive Redstone Data API suite for developers, analysts, and enterprises. Whether you’re building a DeFi dashboard, a wallet, a trading bot, an AI agent or a compliance platform, our Redstone Data APIs provide fast, accurate, and developer-friendly access to the essential onchain data you need.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/redstone#supported-apis)

Supported APIs

[Foundational API\
----------------\
\
Access structured historical blockchain data across 100+ chains using REST APIs. Get token balances, transaction histories, decoded event logs, NFT assets, token holders and more.  \
  \
**Use cases: Wallets, portfolio trackers, crypto accounting & tax tools, and DeFi dashboards.**\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/redstone#mainnet)

| **Chain ID** | `690` |
| **Network Type** | Community Chain |
| **Support Level** | community |
| **Block Explorer** | [Explorer](https://explorer.redstone.xyz/) |
| **Official Website** | [Redstone Website](https://redstone.xyz/) |
| **Native Gas Token** | ETH |

Overview
-----------------------------------------------------------------

GoldRush offers the most comprehensive Fantom Data API suite for developers, analysts, and enterprises. Whether you’re building a DeFi dashboard, a wallet, a trading bot, an AI agent or a compliance platform, our Fantom Data APIs provide fast, accurate, and developer-friendly access to the essential onchain data you need.

###

Supported APIs

[Foundational API\
----------------\
\
Access structured historical blockchain data across 100+ chains using REST APIs. Get token balances, transaction histories, decoded event logs, NFT assets, token holders and more.  \
  \
**Use cases: Wallets, portfolio trackers, crypto accounting & tax tools, and DeFi dashboards.**\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api)

Overview
-------------------------------------------------------------------

GoldRush offers the most comprehensive Unichain Data API suite for developers, analysts, and enterprises. Whether you’re building a DeFi dashboard, a wallet, a trading bot, an AI agent or a compliance platform, our Unichain Data APIs provide fast, accurate, and developer-friendly access to the essential onchain data you need.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/unichain#supported-apis)

Supported APIs

[Foundational API\
----------------\
\
Access structured historical blockchain data across 100+ chains using REST APIs. Get token balances, transaction histories, decoded event logs, NFT assets, token holders and more.  \
  \
**Use cases: Wallets, portfolio trackers, crypto accounting & tax tools, and DeFi dashboards.**\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/unichain#mainnet)

| **Chain ID** | `130` |
| **Network Type** | Frontier Chain |
| **Support Level** | frontier |
| **Block Explorer** | [Unichain Explorer](https://unichain.blockscout.com/) |
| **Official Website** | [Unichain Website](https://www.unichain.org/) |
| **Native Gas Token** | ETH |

Example API Calls

Chain Name (Mainnet)

Chain Name (Unichain Testnet)

Copy

Ask AI

    curl -X GET "https://api.covalenthq.com/v1/unichain-mainnet/address/0xd8dA6BF26964aF9D7eEd9e03E53415D37aA96045/balances_v2/?key=API_KEY"

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/unichain#sdk-usage)

SDK Usage

TypeScript SDK (Mainnet)

TypeScript SDK (Unichain Testnet)

Copy

Ask AI

    import { GoldRushClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    const client = new GoldRushClient("API_KEY");
    const resp = await client.BalanceService.getTokenBalancesForWalletAddress({
        chainName: "unichain-mainnet",
        walletAddress: "0xd8dA6BF26964aF9D7eEd9e03E53415D37aA96045"
    });

        walletAddress: "0xd8dA6BF26964aF9D7eEd9e03E53415D37aA96045"

Overview
-----------------------------------------------------------------------

GoldRush offers the most comprehensive Cronos zkEVM Data API suite for developers, analysts, and enterprises. Whether you’re building a DeFi dashboard, a wallet, a trading bot, an AI agent or a compliance platform, our Cronos zkEVM Data APIs provide fast, accurate, and developer-friendly access to the essential onchain data you need.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/cronos-zkevm#supported-apis)

Supported APIs

[Foundational API\
----------------\
\
Access structured historical blockchain data across 100+ chains using REST APIs. Get token balances, transaction histories, decoded event logs, NFT assets, token holders and more.  \
  \
**Use cases: Wallets, portfolio trackers, crypto accounting & tax tools, and DeFi dashboards.**\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/cronos-zkevm#mainnet)

| **Chain ID** | `388` |
| **Network Type** | Community Chain |
| **Support Level** | community |
| **Block Explorer** | [Explorer](https://explorer.zkevm.cronos.org/) |
| **Official Website** | [Cronos zkEVM Website](https://docs.cronos.org/cronos-zkevm/cronos-zkevm) |
| **Native Gas Token** | zkCRO |

TypeScript SDK (Mainnet)

Copy

Ask AI

    import { GoldRushClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    const client = new GoldRushClient("API_KEY");
    const resp = await client.BalanceService.getTokenBalancesForWalletAddress({
        chainName: "cronos-zkevm-mainnet",
        walletAddress: "0xd8dA6BF26964aF9D7eEd9e03E53415D37aA96045"
    });

Overview
----------------------------------------------------------------

GoldRush offers the most comprehensive Linea Data API suite for developers, analysts, and enterprises. Whether you’re building a DeFi dashboard, a wallet, a trading bot, an AI agent or a compliance platform, our Linea Data APIs provide fast, accurate, and developer-friendly access to the essential onchain data you need.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/linea#supported-apis)

Supported APIs

[Foundational API\
----------------\
\
Access structured historical blockchain data across 100+ chains using REST APIs. Get token balances, transaction histories, decoded event logs, NFT assets, token holders and more.  \
  \
**Use cases: Wallets, portfolio trackers, crypto accounting & tax tools, and DeFi dashboards.**\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/linea#mainnet)

| **Support Level** | frontier |
| **Block Explorer** | [Explorer](https://lineascan.build/) |
| **Official Website** | [Linea Website](https://linea.build/) |
| **Native Gas Token** | ETH |

Overview
--------------------------------------------------------------------

GoldRush offers the most comprehensive ZetaChain Data API suite for developers, analysts, and enterprises. Whether you’re building a DeFi dashboard, a wallet, a trading bot, an AI agent or a compliance platform, our ZetaChain Data APIs provide fast, accurate, and developer-friendly access to the essential onchain data you need.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/zetachain#supported-apis)

Supported APIs

[Foundational API\
----------------\
\
Access structured historical blockchain data across 100+ chains using REST APIs. Get token balances, transaction histories, decoded event logs, NFT assets, token holders and more.  \
  \
**Use cases: Wallets, portfolio trackers, crypto accounting & tax tools, and DeFi dashboards.**\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api)

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/zetachain#mainnet)

| **Support Level** | community |

API Usage

Example API Calls

Chain Name (Mainnet)

Copy

Ask AI

    curl -X GET "https://api.covalenthq.com/v1/zetachain-mainnet/address/0xd8dA6BF26964aF9D7eEd9e03E53415D37aA96045/balances_v2/?key=API_KEY"
    

#### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/zetachain#sdk-usage)

SDK Usage

TypeScript SDK (Mainnet)

Copy

Ask AI

    import { GoldRushClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    const client = new GoldRushClient("API_KEY");
    const resp = await client.BalanceService.getTokenBalancesForWalletAddress({
        chainName: "zetachain-mainnet",
        walletAddress: "0xd8dA6BF26964aF9D7eEd9e03E53415D37aA96045"
    });
