Overview
---------------------------------------------------------------

GoldRush offers the most comprehensive Base Data API suite for developers, analysts, and enterprises. Whether you’re building a DeFi dashboard, a wallet, a trading bot, an AI agent or a compliance platform, our Base Data APIs provide fast, accurate, and developer-friendly access to the essential onchain data you need.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/base#supported-apis)

Supported APIs

[Foundational API\
----------------\
\
Access structured historical blockchain data across 100+ chains using REST APIs. Get token balances, transaction histories, decoded event logs, NFT assets, token holders and more.  \
  \
**Use cases: Wallets, portfolio trackers, crypto accounting & tax tools, and DeFi dashboards.**\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api)
[Streaming API\
-------------\
\
Subscribe to real-time blockchain events with sub-second latency using GraphQL over WebSockets. Track token transfers, DEX activity, wallet movements, and OHLCV candlestick data across fast chains like Base and Solana.  \
  \
**Use cases: Trading bots & dashboards, gaming, and AI Agents.**\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-streaming-api)

Overview

Whether you’re building a DeFi dashboard, a wallet, a trading bot, an AI agent or a compliance platform, our zkSync Era Data APIs provide fast, accurate, and developer-friendly access to the essential onchain data you need.

Overview
----------------------------------------------------------------

GoldRush offers the most comprehensive opBNB Data API suite for developers, analysts, and enterprises. Whether you’re building a DeFi dashboard, a wallet, a trading bot, an AI agent or a compliance platform, our opBNB Data APIs provide fast, accurate, and developer-friendly access to the essential onchain data you need.

### 

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/chains/opbnb#supported-apis)

Supported APIs

[Foundational API\
----------------\
\
Access structured historical blockchain data across 100+ chains using REST APIs. Get token balances, transaction histories, decoded event logs, NFT assets, token holders and more.  \
  \
**Use cases: Wallets, portfolio trackers, crypto accounting & tax tools, and DeFi dashboards.**\
\
Read docs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api)

    import { GoldRushClient } from "@covalenthq/client-sdk";
    
    const ApiServices = async () => {
        const client = new GoldRushClient("YOUR_API_KEY");
        const resp = await client.BaseService.getAddressActivity({chainName: "chainName", walletAddress: "walletAddress"});
        console.log(resp.data);
    };
    
    ApiServices();

Credit Cost
-----------

0.5 per call

Processing
----------

Realtime

Related guides

[Calculate Crypto Cost Basis and Capital Gains with GoldRush](https://goldrush.dev/guides/calculate-crypto-cost-basis-and-capital-gains-with-covalent)
[DIY - Build Your Own Crypto Tax Calculator with Google Sheets](https://goldrush.dev/guides/diy-build-your-own-crypto-tax-calculator-with-google-sheets)

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-address-activity#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-address-activity#parameter-wallet-address)

walletAddress

string

required

The requested wallet address. Passing in an `ENS`, `RNS`, `Lens Handle`, or an `Unstoppable Domain` resolves automatically.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-address-activity#parameter-testnets)

testnets

boolean

Set to true to include testnets with activity in the response. By default, it's set to `false` and only returns mainnet activity.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-address-activity#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-address-activity#response-address)

address

string

The requested address.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-address-activity#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

[Authentication](https://goldrush.dev/docs/goldrush-foundational-api/authentication)
[Get multichain balances](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/cross-chain/get-allchains-balances)

Credit Cost
-----------

0.1 per item

Processing
----------

Realtime

Requests that return status 200 and no data cost 0.1 credits.

Related guides

[What are Deterministic Wallets and How They Work?](https://goldrush.dev/guides/what-are-deterministic-wallets-and-how-they-work)

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balances-for-hd-address#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balances-for-hd-address#parameter-wallet-address)

walletAddress

string

required

The extended public key (xPub/yPub/zPub) of the HD wallet.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balances-for-hd-address#parameter-quote-currency)

quote-currency

string

The currency to convert the balance to. Supports `USD`, `CAD`, `EUR`, etc.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balances-for-hd-address#response-address)

address

string

The extended public key (xPub/yPub/zPub) or HD wallet address.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balances-for-hd-address#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `20090103`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balances-for-hd-address#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `btc-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balances-for-hd-address#response-chain-tip-height)

chain\_tip\_height

integer

The latest block height of the blockchain at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balances-for-hd-address#response-chain-tip-signed-at)

chain\_tip\_signed\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp of the latest signed block at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balances-for-hd-address#response-quote-currency)

quote\_currency

string

The requested quote currency eg: `USD`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balances-for-hd-address#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balances-for-hd-address#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of HD wallet balance items, each containing derived addresses and balances.

Show child attributes

[Get Bitcoin balance for non-HD address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-bitcoin-balance-for-address)

Credit Cost
-----------

1 per call

Processing
----------

Realtime

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-bitcoin-balance-for-address#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-bitcoin-balance-for-address#parameter-wallet-address)

walletAddress

string

required

Only Bitcoin non-HD addresses are supported.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-bitcoin-balance-for-address#parameter-quote-currency)

quote-currency

string

The currency to convert. Supports `USD`, `CAD`, `EUR`, `SGD`, `INR`, `JPY`, `VND`, `CNY`, `KRW`, `RUB`, `TRY`, `NGN`, `ARS`, `AUD`, `CHF`, and `GBP`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-bitcoin-balance-for-address#parameter-block-height)

block-height

integer

Ending block to define a block range. Omitting this parameter defaults to the latest block height.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-bitcoin-balance-for-address#parameter-date)

date

string

Ending date to define a block range (YYYY-MM-DD). Omitting this parameter defaults to the current date.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-bitcoin-balance-for-address#response-address)

address

string

The requested address.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-bitcoin-balance-for-address#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-bitcoin-balance-for-address#response-quote-currency)

quote\_currency

string

The requested quote currency eg: `USD`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-bitcoin-balance-for-address#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-bitcoin-balance-for-address#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-bitcoin-balance-for-address#response-chain-tip-height)

chain\_tip\_height

integer

The latest block height of the blockchain at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-bitcoin-balance-for-address#response-chain-tip-signed-at)

chain\_tip\_signed\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp of the latest signed block at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-bitcoin-balance-for-address#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

string

header

page-size

integer

page-number

integer

0-indexed page number to begin pagination.

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-resolved-address-for-registered-address#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-resolved-address-for-registered-address#parameter-chain-name)

chainName

string

required

The chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-resolved-address-for-registered-address#parameter-wallet-address)

walletAddress

string

required

The requested address. Passing in an `ENS`, `RNS`, `Lens Handle`, or an `Unstoppable Domain` resolves automatically.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-resolved-address-for-registered-address#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-resolved-address-for-registered-address#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-resolved-address-for-registered-address#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-resolved-address-for-registered-address#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Credit Cost
-----------

0.5 per call

Processing
----------

Realtime

Not supported on non-EVM chains such as Bitcoin and Solana.

Related guides

[Building a Web3 Portfolio Tracker with the GoldRush API](https://goldrush.dev/guides/building-a-web3-portfolio-tracker-with-the-covalent-api)

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-native-token-balance#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-native-token-balance#parameter-chain-name)

chainName

string

required

The chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-native-token-balance#parameter-wallet-address)

walletAddress

string

required

The requested address. Passing in an `ENS`, `RNS`, `Lens Handle`, or an `Unstoppable Domain` resolves automatically.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-native-token-balance#parameter-quote-currency)

quote-currency

string

The currency to convert. Supports `USD`, `CAD`, `EUR`, `SGD`, `INR`, `JPY`, `VND`, `CNY`, `KRW`, `RUB`, `TRY`, `NGN`, `ARS`, `AUD`, `CHF`, and `GBP`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-native-token-balance#parameter-block-height)

block-height

integer

Ending block to define a block range. Omitting this parameter defaults to the latest block height.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-native-token-balance#response-address)

address

string

The requested address.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-native-token-balance#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-native-token-balance#response-quote-currency)

quote\_currency

string

The requested quote currency eg: `USD`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-native-token-balance#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-native-token-balance#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-native-token-balance#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Credit Cost
-----------

1 per call

Processing
----------

Batch

Supports a comma separated list of token contract addresses.If no date range is provided, the spot price (with a 5 minute refresh) is provided.

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-historical-token-prices#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-historical-token-prices#parameter-chain-name)

chainName

string

required

The chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-historical-token-prices#parameter-quote-currency)

quoteCurrency

string

required

The currency to convert. Supports `USD`, `CAD`, `EUR`, `SGD`, `INR`, `JPY`, `VND`, `CNY`, `KRW`, `RUB`, `TRY`, `NGN`, `ARS`, `AUD`, `CHF`, and `GBP`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-historical-token-prices#parameter-contract-address)

contractAddress

string

required

Contract address for the token. Passing in an `ENS`, `RNS`, `Lens Handle`, or an `Unstoppable Domain` resolves automatically. Supports multiple contract addresses separated by commas.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-historical-token-prices#parameter-from)

from

string

The start day of the historical price range (YYYY-MM-DD).

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-historical-token-prices#parameter-to)

to

string

The end day of the historical price range (YYYY-MM-DD).

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-historical-token-prices#parameter-prices-at-asc)

prices-at-asc

boolean

Sort the prices in chronological ascending order. By default, it's set to `false` and returns prices in chronological descending order.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-historical-token-prices#response-contract-decimals)

contract\_decimals

integer

Use contract decimals to format the token balance for display purposes - divide the balance by `10^{contract_decimals}`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-historical-token-prices#response-contract-name)

contract\_name

string

The string returned by the `name()` method.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-historical-token-prices#response-contract-ticker-symbol)

contract\_ticker\_symbol

string

The ticker symbol for this contract. This field is set by a developer and non-unique across a network.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-historical-token-prices#response-contract-address)

contract\_address

string

Use the relevant `contract_address` to lookup prices, logos, token transfers, etc.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-historical-token-prices#response-supports-erc)

supports\_erc

string\[\]

A list of supported standard ERC interfaces, eg: `ERC20` and `ERC721`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-historical-token-prices#response-logo-url)

logo\_url

string

The contract logo URL.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-historical-token-prices#response-update-at)

update\_at

string<date-time>

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-historical-token-prices#response-quote-currency)

quote\_currency

string

The requested quote currency eg: `USD`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-historical-token-prices#response-logo-urls)

logo\_urls

object

The contract logo URLs.

Show child attributes

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-historical-token-prices#response-prices)

prices

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-historical-token-prices#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

[Get Bitcoin transactions for non-HD address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-transactions-for-bitcoin-address)
[Get pool spot prices](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-pool-spot-prices)

header

chainName

required

The chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-portfolio-value-over-time#response-quote-currency)

quote\_currency

string

The requested quote currency eg: `USD`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-portfolio-value-over-time#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-portfolio-value-over-time#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-portfolio-value-over-time#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#parameter-chain-name)

chainName

string

required

The chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#parameter-wallet-address)

walletAddress

string

required

The requested address. Passing in an `ENS`, `RNS`, `Lens Handle`, or an `Unstoppable Domain` resolves automatically.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#parameter-quote-currency)

quote-currency

string

The currency to convert. Supports `USD`, `CAD`, `EUR`, `SGD`, `INR`, `JPY`, `VND`, `CNY`, `KRW`, `RUB`, `TRY`, `NGN`, `ARS`, `AUD`, `CHF`, and `GBP`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#parameter-contract-address)

contract-address

string

required

The requested contract address. Passing in an `ENS`, `RNS`, `Lens Handle`, or an `Unstoppable Domain` resolves automatically.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#parameter-starting-block)

starting-block

integer

The block height to start from, defaults to `0`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#parameter-ending-block)

ending-block

integer

The block height to end at, defaults to current block height.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#parameter-page-size)

page-size

integer

Number of items per page. Omitting this parameter defaults to 100.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#parameter-page-number)

page-number

integer

0-indexed page number to begin pagination.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#response-address)

address

string

The requested address.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#response-quote-currency)

quote\_currency

string

The requested quote currency eg: `USD`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#response-chain-tip-height)

chain\_tip\_height

integer

The latest block height of the blockchain at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#response-chain-tip-signed-at)

chain\_tip\_signed\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp of the latest signed block at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-erc20-token-transfers-for-address#response-pagination)

pagination

object

Pagination metadata.

Show child attributes

[Get native token balance for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-native-token-balance)
[Get historical portfolio value over time](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-portfolio-value-over-time)

Credit Cost
-----------

0.1 per call

Processing
----------

Realtime

Base cost is `0.1` credits (e.g. requests that return with status `200` but no items).Calls with `no-logs` cost `0.05` credits/item.The following tracing features each cost `0.05` credits where available on [Foundational Chains](https://goldrush.dev/chains)
:

*   `with-internal` - includes internal transfers/transactions.
*   `with-state` - includes all transaction state changes with before and after values.
*   `with-input-data` - includes the transaction’s input data such as the Method ID.

Currently, tracing features are supported on the following chains:

*   `eth-mainnet`

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-a-transaction#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-a-transaction#parameter-chain-name)

chainName

string

required

The chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-a-transaction#parameter-tx-hash)

txHash

string

required

The transaction hash.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-a-transaction#parameter-quote-currency)

quote-currency

string

The currency to convert. Supports `USD`, `CAD`, `EUR`, `SGD`, `INR`, `JPY`, `VND`, `CNY`, `KRW`, `RUB`, `TRY`, `NGN`, `ARS`, `AUD`, `CHF`, and `GBP`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-a-transaction#parameter-no-logs)

no-logs

boolean

Omit log events.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-a-transaction#parameter-with-internal)

with-internal

boolean

Whether to include internal transfers/transactions.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-a-transaction#parameter-with-state)

with-state

boolean

Whether to include all transaction state changes with before and after values.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-a-transaction#parameter-with-input-data)

with-input-data

boolean

Whether to include the transaction's input data such as the Method ID.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-a-transaction#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-a-transaction#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-a-transaction#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-a-transaction#response-chain-tip-height)

chain\_tip\_height

integer

The latest block height of the blockchain at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-a-transaction#response-chain-tip-signed-at)

chain\_tip\_signed\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp of the latest signed block at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-a-transaction#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

[Get token holders as of any block height (v2)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-token-holders-as-of-any-block-height-v2)
[Get transaction summary for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-transaction-summary-for-address)

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block-by-page#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block-by-page#parameter-chain-name)

chainName

string

required

The chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block-by-page#parameter-block-height)

blockHeight

integer

required

The requested block height. Also accepts `latest` to get latest block.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block-by-page#parameter-page)

page

integer

required

The requested 0-indexed page number.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block-by-page#parameter-quote-currency)

quote-currency

string

The currency to convert. Supports `USD`, `CAD`, `EUR`, `SGD`, `INR`, `JPY`, `VND`, `CNY`, `KRW`, `RUB`, `TRY`, `NGN`, `ARS`, `AUD`, `CHF`, and `GBP`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block-by-page#parameter-no-logs)

no-logs

boolean

Omit log events.

Successful response

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block-by-page#response-chain-name)

string

Credit Cost
-----------

0.1 per item

Processing
----------

Realtime

Returns the same results as the first timebucket for an address in the [Get recent transactions](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api/transactions/get-recent-transactions-for-address-v3/)
 endpoint.Requests that return status 200 and no data cost 0.1 credits.Enabling `no-logs` reduces request cost to 0.05 per item.

Related guides

[Introducing Transactions V3 APIs](https://goldrush.dev/guides/introducing-transactions-v3-apis)
[Comparing GoldRush’s Transactions API to RPC Providers](https://goldrush.dev/guides/comparing-covalent-s-transactions-api-to-rpc-providers)
[How to Get Transaction History for an Address on Ethereum](https://goldrush.dev/guides/how-to-get-transaction-history-for-an-address-on-ethereum)

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-earliest-transactions-for-address-v3#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-earliest-transactions-for-address-v3#parameter-chain-name)

chainName

string

required

The chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-earliest-transactions-for-address-v3#parameter-wallet-address)

walletAddress

string

required

The requested address. Passing in an `ENS`, `RNS`, `Lens Handle`, or an `Unstoppable Domain` resolves automatically.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-earliest-transactions-for-address-v3#parameter-quote-currency)

quote-currency

string

The currency to convert. Supports `USD`, `CAD`, `EUR`, `SGD`, `INR`, `JPY`, `VND`, `CNY`, `KRW`, `RUB`, `TRY`, `NGN`, `ARS`, `AUD`, `CHF`, and `GBP`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-earliest-transactions-for-address-v3#parameter-no-logs)

no-logs

boolean

Omit log events.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-earliest-transactions-for-address-v3#response-address)

address

string

The requested address.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-earliest-transactions-for-address-v3#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-earliest-transactions-for-address-v3#response-quote-currency)

quote\_currency

string

The requested quote currency eg: `USD`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-earliest-transactions-for-address-v3#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-earliest-transactions-for-address-v3#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-earliest-transactions-for-address-v3#response-chain-tip-height)

chain\_tip\_height

integer

The latest block height of the blockchain at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-earliest-transactions-for-address-v3#response-chain-tip-signed-at)

chain\_tip\_signed\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp of the latest signed block at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-earliest-transactions-for-address-v3#response-complete)

complete

boolean

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-earliest-transactions-for-address-v3#response-current-bucket)

current\_bucket

integer

The current bucket of the response.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-earliest-transactions-for-address-v3#response-links)

links

object

Show child attributes

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-earliest-transactions-for-address-v3#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-a-block#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-a-block#parameter-chain-name)

chainName

string

required

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-a-block#parameter-block-height)

blockHeight

string

required

The block height or `latest` for the latest block available.

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-a-block#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block#parameter-chain-name)

chainName

string

required

The chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block#parameter-block-hash)

blockHash

string

required

The requested block hash.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block#parameter-quote-currency)

quote-currency

string

The currency to convert. Supports `USD`, `CAD`, `EUR`, `SGD`, `INR`, `JPY`, `VND`, `CNY`, `KRW`, `RUB`, `TRY`, `NGN`, `ARS`, `AUD`, `CHF`, and `GBP`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block#parameter-no-logs)

no-logs

boolean

Omit log events.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block#response-chain-tip-height)

chain\_tip\_height

integer

The latest block height of the blockchain at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block#response-chain-tip-signed-at)

chain\_tip\_signed\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp of the latest signed block at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

[Get all transactions in a block by page (v3)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block-by-page)
 [Get NFTs for address](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/nft/get-nfts-for-address)

Credit Cost
-----------

0.1 per item

Processing
----------

Realtime

This endpoint returns paginated transactions, starting with the earliest transactions on page 0. For the most recent transactions, refer to the [Get recent transactions for address (v3)](https://www.covalenthq.com/docs/api/transactions/get-recent-transactions-for-address-v3/)
 endpoint.Requests that return status 200 and no data cost 0.1 credits.Enabling `no-logs` reduces request cost to 0.05 per item.

Related guides

[Introducing Transactions V3 APIs](https://goldrush.dev/guides/introducing-transactions-v3-apis)
[Calculate Crypto Cost Basis and Capital Gains with GoldRush](https://goldrush.dev/guides/calculate-crypto-cost-basis-and-capital-gains-with-covalent)
[Discover Your Ethereum Gas Consumption with the GoldRush API](https://goldrush.dev/guides/ethereum-gas-consumption)
[How Token Gating and Membership dApps Use the GoldRush API](https://goldrush.dev/guides/how-token-gating-dapps-use-the-covalent-api)
[Comparing GoldRush’s Transactions API to RPC Providers](https://goldrush.dev/guides/comparing-covalent-s-transactions-api-to-rpc-providers)
[How to Get Transaction History for an Address on Ethereum](https://goldrush.dev/guides/how-to-get-transaction-history-for-an-address-on-ethereum)
[Getting Started with the GoldRush SDK](https://goldrush.dev/guides/getting-started-with-the-covalent-sdk)
[How to Use Covalent’s Wallet Transaction Analysis Tool](https://goldrush.dev/guides/how-to-use-covalent-s-wallet-transaction-analysis-tool)

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-paginated-transactions-for-address-v3#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-paginated-transactions-for-address-v3#parameter-chain-name)

chainName

string

required

The chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-paginated-transactions-for-address-v3#parameter-wallet-address)

walletAddress

string

required

The requested address. Passing in an `ENS`, `RNS`, `Lens Handle`, or an `Unstoppable Domain` resolves automatically.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-paginated-transactions-for-address-v3#parameter-page)

page

integer

required

The requested page, 0-indexed.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-paginated-transactions-for-address-v3#parameter-quote-currency)

quote-currency

string

The currency to convert. Supports `USD`, `CAD`, `EUR`, `SGD`, `INR`, `JPY`, `VND`, `CNY`, `KRW`, `RUB`, `TRY`, `NGN`, `ARS`, `AUD`, `CHF`, and `GBP`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-paginated-transactions-for-address-v3#parameter-no-logs)

no-logs

boolean

Omit log events.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-paginated-transactions-for-address-v3#parameter-block-signed-at-asc)

block-signed-at-asc

boolean

Sort the transactions in ascending chronological order. By default, it's set to `false` and returns transactions in descending chronological order.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-paginated-transactions-for-address-v3#response-address)

address

string

The requested address.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-paginated-transactions-for-address-v3#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-paginated-transactions-for-address-v3#response-quote-currency)

quote\_currency

string

The requested quote currency eg: `USD`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-paginated-transactions-for-address-v3#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-paginated-transactions-for-address-v3#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-paginated-transactions-for-address-v3#response-chain-tip-height)

chain\_tip\_height

integer

The latest block height of the blockchain at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-paginated-transactions-for-address-v3#response-chain-tip-signed-at)

chain\_tip\_signed\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp of the latest signed block at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-paginated-transactions-for-address-v3#response-current-page)

current\_page

integer

The current page of the response.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-paginated-transactions-for-address-v3#response-links)

links

object

Show child attributes

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-paginated-transactions-for-address-v3#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

[Get bulk time bucket transactions for address (v3)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-time-bucket-transactions-for-address-v3)

        const resp = await client.TransactionService.getRecentTransactionsForAddress({chainName: "chainName", walletAddress: "walletAddress"});

    };

string

The requested quote currency eg: `USD`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-recent-transactions-for-address-v3#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-recent-transactions-for-address-v3#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-recent-transactions-for-address-v3#response-chain-tip-height)

chain\_tip\_height

integer

The latest block height of the blockchain at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-recent-transactions-for-address-v3#response-chain-tip-signed-at)

chain\_tip\_signed\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp of the latest signed block at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-recent-transactions-for-address-v3#response-current-page)

current\_page

integer

The current page of the response.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-recent-transactions-for-address-v3#response-links)

links

object

Show child attributes

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-recent-transactions-for-address-v3#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

Credit Cost
-----------

0.1 per item

Processing
----------

Realtime

Requests that return status 200 and no data cost 0.1 credits.Enabling `no-logs` reduces request cost to 0.05 per item.

Related guides

[Scaling Transactions API with Time Buckets](https://goldrush.dev/guides/scaling-transactions-time-buckets)
[Introducing Transactions V3 APIs](https://goldrush.dev/guides/introducing-transactions-v3-apis)
[How to Get the Earliest Transaction History for an Address on Ethereum](https://goldrush.dev/guides/how-to-get-the-earliest-transaction-history-for-an-address-on-ethereum)
[Comparing GoldRush’s Transactions API to RPC Providers](https://goldrush.dev/guides/comparing-covalent-s-transactions-api-to-rpc-providers)

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-time-bucket-transactions-for-address-v3#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-time-bucket-transactions-for-address-v3#parameter-chain-name)

chainName

string

required

The chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-time-bucket-transactions-for-address-v3#parameter-wallet-address)

walletAddress

string

required

The requested address. Passing in an `ENS`, `RNS`, `Lens Handle`, or an `Unstoppable Domain` resolves automatically.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-time-bucket-transactions-for-address-v3#parameter-time-bucket)

timeBucket

integer

required

The 0-indexed 15-minute time bucket. E.g. 27 Feb 2023 05:23 GMT = 1677475383 (Unix time). 1677475383/900=1863861 timeBucket.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-time-bucket-transactions-for-address-v3#parameter-quote-currency)

quote-currency

string

The currency to convert. Supports `USD`, `CAD`, `EUR`, `SGD`, `INR`, `JPY`, `VND`, `CNY`, `KRW`, `RUB`, `TRY`, `NGN`, `ARS`, `AUD`, `CHF`, and `GBP`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-time-bucket-transactions-for-address-v3#parameter-no-logs)

no-logs

boolean

Omit log events.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-time-bucket-transactions-for-address-v3#response-address)

address

string

The requested address.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-time-bucket-transactions-for-address-v3#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-time-bucket-transactions-for-address-v3#response-quote-currency)

quote\_currency

string

The requested quote currency eg: `USD`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-time-bucket-transactions-for-address-v3#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-time-bucket-transactions-for-address-v3#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-time-bucket-transactions-for-address-v3#response-chain-tip-height)

chain\_tip\_height

integer

The latest block height of the blockchain at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-time-bucket-transactions-for-address-v3#response-chain-tip-signed-at)

chain\_tip\_signed\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp of the latest signed block at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-time-bucket-transactions-for-address-v3#response-complete)

complete

boolean

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-time-bucket-transactions-for-address-v3#response-current-bucket)

current\_bucket

integer

The current bucket of the response.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-time-bucket-transactions-for-address-v3#response-links)

links

object

Show child attributes

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-time-bucket-transactions-for-address-v3#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

[Get paginated transactions for address (v3)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-paginated-transactions-for-address-v3)
[Get all transactions in a block by page (v3)](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/transactions/get-all-transactions-in-a-block-by-page)

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-block-heights#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-block-heights#parameter-chain-name)

chainName

string

required

The chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-block-heights#parameter-start-date)

startDate

string

required

The start date in YYYY-MM-DD format.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-block-heights#parameter-end-date)

endDate

string

required

The end date in YYYY-MM-DD format or `latest` for the latest block available.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-block-heights#parameter-page-size)

page-size

integer

Number of items per page. Omitting this parameter defaults to 100.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-block-heights#parameter-page-number)

page-number

integer

0-indexed page number to begin pagination.

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-block-heights#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-block-heights#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-block-heights#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-block-heights#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-block-heights#response-pagination)

pagination

object

Pagination metadata.

Credit Cost
-----------

1 per call

Processing
----------

Batch

Currently support these event types: `erc20` token transfers, `nativetokens` transfer, and `uniswapv3` swap events.

Related guides

[How to Fetch Onchain Gas Prices and Estimate Gas Costs](https://goldrush.dev/guides/how-to-fetch-gas-prices-and-estimate-gas-costs)

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-gas-prices#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-gas-prices#parameter-chain-name)

chainName

string

required

The chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-gas-prices#parameter-event-type)

eventType

string

required

The desired event type to retrieve gas prices for. Supports `erc20` transfer events, `uniswapv3` swap events and `nativetokens` transfers.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-gas-prices#parameter-quote-currency)

quote-currency

string

The currency to convert. Supports `USD`, `CAD`, `EUR`, `SGD`, `INR`, `JPY`, `VND`, `CNY`, `KRW`, `RUB`, `TRY`, `NGN`, `ARS`, `AUD`, `CHF`, and `GBP`.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-gas-prices#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-gas-prices#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-gas-prices#response-quote-currency)

quote\_currency

string

The requested quote currency eg: `USD`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-gas-prices#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-gas-prices#response-event-type)

event\_type

string

The requested event type.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-gas-prices#response-gas-quote-rate)

gas\_quote\_rate

number<double>

The exchange rate for the requested quote currency.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-gas-prices#response-base-fee)

base\_fee

string

b;The lowest gas fee for the latest block height.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-gas-prices#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

[Get pool spot prices](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-pool-spot-prices)
[Get logs](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-logs)

Related guides

[How to Fetch User Operations (UserOps) for a Specific Wallet Address](https://goldrush.dev/guides/how-to-fetch-user-operations-userops-for-a-specific-wallet-address)
[What are Event Logs?](https://goldrush.dev/guides/evm-event-logs)

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash#parameter-chain-name)

chainName

string

required

The chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash#parameter-topic-hash)

topicHash

string

required

The endpoint will return event logs that contain this topic hash.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash#parameter-starting-block)

starting-block

integer

The first block to retrieve log events with. Accepts decimals, hexadecimals, or the strings `earliest` and `latest`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash#parameter-ending-block)

ending-block

string

The last block to retrieve log events with. Accepts decimals, hexadecimals, or the strings `earliest` and `latest`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash#parameter-secondary-topics)

secondary-topics

string

Additional topic hash(es) to filter on - padded & unpadded address fields are supported. Separate multiple topics with a comma.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash#parameter-page-size)

page-size

integer

Number of items per page. Omitting this parameter defaults to 100.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash#parameter-page-number)

page-number

integer

0-indexed page number to begin pagination.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash#response-chain-tip-height)

chain\_tip\_height

integer

The latest block height of the blockchain at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash#response-chain-tip-signed-at)

chain\_tip\_signed\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp of the latest signed block at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/utility/get-log-events-by-topic-hash#response-pagination)

pagination

object

Pagination metadata.

Show child attributes

Credit Cost
-----------

1 per call

Processing
----------

Realtime

Supported on all [Foundational Chains](https://goldrush.dev/chains/)
.

#### Authorizations

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Bearer authentication header of the form: `Bearer <token>`, where `<token>` is your GoldRush API Key.

#### Path Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address#parameter-chain-name)

chainName

string

required

The chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address#parameter-wallet-address)

walletAddress

string

required

The requested address. Passing in an `ENS`, `RNS`, `Lens Handle`, or an `Unstoppable Domain` resolves automatically.

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address#parameter-quote-currency)

quote-currency

string

The currency to convert. Supports `USD`, `CAD`, `EUR`, `SGD`, `INR`, `JPY`, `VND`, `CNY`, `KRW`, `RUB`, `TRY`, `NGN`, `ARS`, `AUD`, `CHF`, and `GBP`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address#parameter-no-spam)

no-spam

boolean

If `true`, the suspected spam tokens are removed. Supported on all Foundational Chains.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address#parameter-block-height)

block-height

integer

Ending block to define a block range. Omitting this parameter defaults to the latest block height.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address#parameter-date)

date

string

Ending date to define a block range (YYYY-MM-DD). Omitting this parameter defaults to the current date.

#### Response

200 - application/json

Successful response

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address#response-address)

address

string

The requested address.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address#response-updated-at)

updated\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp when the response was generated. Useful to show data staleness to users.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address#response-quote-currency)

quote\_currency

string

The requested quote currency eg: `USD`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address#response-chain-id)

chain\_id

integer

The requested chain ID eg: `1`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address#response-chain-name)

chain\_name

string

The requested chain name eg: `eth-mainnet`.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address#response-chain-tip-height)

chain\_tip\_height

integer

The latest block height of the blockchain at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address#response-chain-tip-signed-at)

chain\_tip\_signed\_at

string<date-time>

The timestamp of the latest signed block at the time this response was provided.

[​](https://goldrush.dev/docs/api-reference/foundational-api/balances/get-historical-token-balances-for-address#response-items)

items

object\[\]

List of response items.

Show child attributes
